  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }
  //]]>
</script>

  <span id="freeText13344157799977353434" style="display:none"><b>Number-one New York Times best-selling author J.R. Ward's thrilling new novel in the Black Dagger Brotherhood series.</b><br /><br />Payne, twin sister of Vishous, is cut from the same dark, seductive cloth as her brother. Imprisoned for eons by their mother, the Scribe Virgin, she finally frees herself - only to face a devastating injury.<br /><br />Manuel Manello, M.D., is drafted by the Brotherhood to save her as only he can - but when the human surgeon and the vampire warrior meet, their two worlds collide in the face of their undeniable passion. With so much working against them, can love prove stronger than the birthright and the biology that separates them?<br /><br /><i>18 hours and 37 minutes.</i></span>

<div id="review_104182030" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/104182030" />
    <a title="Mel" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2295424-mel"><img alt="Mel" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1305638929p2/2295424.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/104182030?book_show_action=true">May 25, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mel" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mel" href="/user/show/2295424-mel">Mel</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2295424-mel?shelf=e-book">e-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2295424-mel?shelf=2011">2011</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer104182030" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15031186825822127732">Lover Unleashed is the tenth book in the Black Dagger Brotherhood universe and it’s about Payne and Manny finding love. To me, it’s also… a huge disappointment.<br/>Why? Because I feel that the loyal fans got screwed over. The way Ward just blatantly rewrites history, disregards her own world's rules and has characters act completely out of character... It's insulting really! <br/><br/>I’ve been looking forward to this book like crazy. Eventhough I wasn’t interested in Payne and Manny’s story at all. In fact: </span>
  <span id="freeText15031186825822127732" style="display:none">Lover Unleashed is the tenth book in the Black Dagger Brotherhood universe and it’s about Payne and Manny finding love. To me, it’s also… a huge disappointment.<br />Why? Because I feel that the loyal fans got screwed over. The way Ward just blatantly rewrites history, disregards her own world's rules and has characters act completely out of character... It's insulting really! <br /><br />I’ve been looking forward to this book like crazy. Eventhough I wasn’t interested in Payne and Manny’s story at all. In fact: I was fully expecting to hastily flip through the Payne/Manny bits, just to get to the good stuff: V’s downward spiral and the Qhuinn/Blay drama. At the end though: the love story between Payne and Manny was the best part of the book. And that’s saying something. <br /><br />If this book emphasizes one thing, it is that Ward needs a new editor. Sure, the current one cries and raves about everything Ward says. But I thought an editor’s job was to actually, oh I don’t know… <i>edit</i>? Correct mistakes? Make sure the story flows well? Secure continuity in characters, actions and events? Check the time line? <br />Nope, no such thing. But hey: I bet she’s great at nodding her head. <br /><br />Basically, Lover Unleashed is two big story lines and three mini story lines put together.<br />The two bigger story lines revolve around Payne &amp; Manny and V, Jane &amp; Butch. The three mini story lines are about Qhuinn &amp; Blay, the Band of Bastards and about <s>the next Fallen Angels book</s> Jose de la Cruz and his new partner. <br /><br />(Minor spoilers from here on:) <br /><br /><u>The good: </u><br />- Manny: before this story I was simply not invested enough to care about what happened to the guy. Over the course of this book, however, I grew to really like him. Ward described him as ‘a metrosexual motherfucker’ but he’s really a regular alpha guy who’s not afraid to let his lady have the limelight. <br />- The Band of Bastards: I loved the itty grittiness of them. Xcor is really intriguing, Zypher needs a long way to be redeemed (somehow that’s sexy) and Throe, what can I say: I wish my friend Tara hadn’t called dibbs cause I wants him! <br />- Butch: I just love Butch. <br /><br /><u>The bad: </u><br />- Vishous' downward spiral: spelled C-O-N-T-R-I-V-E-D to me. The angst was completely forged and supported only by out of character actions by both Jane and Vishous. Plus: the whole thing was based on a faulty premise: the mating ceremony between V an Jane supposedly not having taken place. Say what?!? <br />- The Butch story line: yes I love Butch, but I can’t get over the fact what a missed chance this was for Ward to write more about our favorite ex-human with his chipped tooth (which mysteriously turned into a capped tooth in this book…). In a story which features Vishous, Manny and Jose de la Cruz, you’d expect more about him! And I’m not even going to mention the missed opportunity concerning the V/Butch quality time. Such a waste… <br />- Payne: <i> ‘the female warrior’.</i> Right… Payne is what Xhex haters would want her to be: a tough chick disguised in a Chosen package. We are told she’s tough and she holds her ground. We just don’t really see it. Also: this Payne didn’t resemble the girl we met in Lover Avenged. She felt more like Marissa or Cormia. Only with dark hair. <br />-Layla: like Payne, there was a change of character in Layla. Ward decided to give her a backbone this book. It just doesn’t match her behavior from last books... or this book, really. I feel like it’s an attempt from Ward to make us like Layla. Mission failed on my account. <br />- Jane: okay now, I’ll admit; I’m not the biggest Jane fan. I have problems with her status as Super Shellan and I get annoyed by the way Ward just needs to drive the point home (again and again) about how smart Jane is. And well.. in this book we were told (again and again) how smart the super doc was. Too bad she didn’t actually show it in her behavior. <br />- the blending POVs: maybe it’s me, maybe it’s due to all the Wardisms, but all the inner POVs are starting to sound alike. Open up a random chapter and it’s almost impossible to differentiate who’s talking or thinking anymore. <br />- the ending: if felt rushed and unfinished. Twenty pages is too short to wrap up five story lines!<br /><br /><u>The ugly: </u><br />- No John Matthew. At all. I missed him. <br />- The Jose de la Cruz and Thomas DelVecchio story line: I found it really interesting… right up to the point where I realized it didn’t serve any purpose in expanding Butch’s or the Bastards’ story line. It’s just one big infomercial for the next Fallen Angels book. <br />- The castration of Xcor: here we have an intriguing, morally ambiguous hero with lots of potential. And Ward turns him into a sap near the end of the book. Why?!?<br />- The revelation of what Qhuinn saw on the door of the Fade: if this is going where I think it’s going, then I’m seriously considering a series boycott. One word: <i>ridiculous</i>. <br /><br /><u>The hysterical: </u><br />- The Wardisms: is it me or are they getting worse each book? The number one Wardism for this book has to be ‘going/getting vertical’. Another favorite word: ‘kibitzer’. There was also lots of extrapolation going on. <br />- Ehlena: she was the Super Extra. I think she was mentioned over forty times in the book. She didn’t utter one word though. <br />- Manny’s perpetual hard ons: We get it: he’s excited. But it got a bit silly towards the ending…<br /><br />Now, I’ll be the last to say that the BDB series has always been perfect. It’s a bit over the top, sometimes silly, riddled with continuity mistakes. But until now Ward managed to compensate all this with great story telling, excitement and entertainment.<br />This time around I just didn't feel it. The main story line was okay, but the secondary story lines were either contrived (V/Jane/Butch), lacking of any substance (Qhuinn/Blay) or completely unnecessary (De La Cruz/Veck).<br />It’s still good for the genre, but it’s certainly my least favorite in the BDB series. A mere 2,5 stars.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15031186825822127732" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer863307931" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer304618721229432183"><b>4 Was this Payne's book or V's? Stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/tumblr_lwqva829xS1qbigl6_zpslsnw7evl.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491578655ra/22425019.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_lwqva829xS1qbigl6_zpslsnw7evl.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b> Spoilers</b><br/><br/>First Read 2014<br/>Reread 4/7/2017<br/><br/><b>It finally happened, he thought as he burrowed under his shirt and took hold of his heavy cross. All his life he'd wondered why he'd never fallen in love, and now he knew: He'd been waiting for this moment, this woman, this time. The female is mine, he thought.-Manny</b><br/><br/>Lover Unleashed the 9th book in the BDB series was a good read but I was a little confused as to whose book it was. I mean was this Payne and Manny's boo</span>
  <span id="freeText304618721229432183" style="display:none"><b>4 Was this Payne's book or V's? Stars</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/tumblr_lwqva829xS1qbigl6_zpslsnw7evl.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491578655ra/22425019.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lwqva829xS1qbigl6_zpslsnw7evl.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b> Spoilers</b><br><br>First Read 2014<br>Reread 4/7/2017<br><br><b>It finally happened, he thought as he burrowed under his shirt and took hold of his heavy cross. All his life he'd wondered why he'd never fallen in love, and now he knew: He'd been waiting for this moment, this woman, this time. The female is mine, he thought.-Manny</b><br><br>Lover Unleashed the 9th book in the BDB series was a good read but I was a little confused as to whose book it was. I mean was this Payne and Manny's book or V and Jane's. Because even though this is suppose to be about Payne and Manny, V and Jane's drama took up most of this book. I will be honest I liked V a lot in his book but in this book I was so upset with him. I am trying to understand were V is coming from with all his past abuses. I feel like he was unloyal to his Shellan Jane every time he thought about Butch in a sexual way or like in this book he was thinking back to his past Dom sex life and it seemed like he missed it. Enough that Jane and Butch wondered if he would cheat on her. I mean WTF? A bonded male should never even think about being with another not even for a minute. It felt like a betrayal of their love. So V really let me down in this book. Though he pulled his shit together in the end I didn't like seeing him feel that way in the first place. It made me lose a little respect for him that he would even question his love for Jane. And man I felt so damn bad for Jane in this book. <br><br><b> And the last thing he saw before he checked out of the Conscious Inn &amp; Suites was Jane's head whipping around in a panic. In her eyes was stark terror, as if the single worst thing that she could imagine was him in agony....And that was when he knew that he still loved her.-V </b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/9774471_zpsw4fsvsl8.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491578655ra/22425020.gif" alt=" photo 9774471_zpsw4fsvsl8.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Anyone but her. She heard him say that over and over again, saw his ashen face and his icy eyes and the way he had closed her out. Funny ... the eternity she'd been granted had always seemed like the grandest blessing. Until she pictured going aeons without the man she loved. Now it was a curse. Where would she go? She couldn't very well continue at the compound. Not if they were estranged like this.-Jane</b><br><br>Why did he even have to question if he still loved her. He is bonded that isn't suppose to go away. I just really didn't like it. I also didn't like the fact that Payne and Manny took a backseat in this book. Their story was out shined by V's shit. I really liked both Payne and Manny. I thought they were cute and sexy together and I would have loved more time with them. Seeing as this was suppose to be their book and all. I enjoyed all the parts about Manny and Payne. I loved that Payne was her own person. She was strong, a fighter, and she was up front and honest. Manny was great too. He may have been human but he was strong in his own right. He stood up to the brothers especially V, and he was totally comfortable in his own skin. He didn't want to become a vampire like Butch. He was just fine with being himself. <br><br><b>"I am the daughter of a god, Manuel. A deity. That glow you call forth from me? It is her very essence as an entity. That is what she is. As for my father? He was nothing but a sadistic bastard who imparted unto me the urge to kill - that was his 'gift.' And do you want to know what I did with it? Do you?" She was aware that her voice was rising but was singularly disinclined to quiet herself. "I killed him, Manuel. And for that crime against mine bloodline, for that offense against the standards of behavior for females, I was imprisoned and held for centuries. So you are too right. Go - and do it now. It is for the best. But do not think that I fit in here any better than you do."-Payne</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/Payneand%20Manny_zpsn9zlksz5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491578655i/22425018._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo Payneand Manny_zpsn9zlksz5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>You are beautiful and sexy and I don't know what the hell your mother or anyone else is doing comparing you to anything or anybody. Nothing comes close to you ... on any level."-Manny</b><br><br>Overall I enjoyed this book but would have liked more Manny/ Payne and less Jane/V. I liked finding out Butch and Manny are half brothers. I really liked the introduction of Xcor and the Band of Bastards. Am I the only one that thought it was hot as shit when Throe and Xcor tag-teamed the prostitute? OMG who would have thought prostitute sex would be so damn hot! I am looking forward to the Xcor plot. I just loved Blay in this book. I am so glad he was doing what was best for him. I liked that he moved on instead of sitting around like a kicked puppy hurting every time he seen Qhuinn with someone else. I have to say I don't feel one bit sorry for Qhuinn. I know he is a lot of fans favorite but not mine. The fact of the matter is he sat there ripping out Blay's heart having sex with everyone he could right in front of Blay, knowing Blay was in love with him. Now he is all "poor me" I love Blay and he is with another. Well Qhuinn could have Blay if he just grew some damn balls. No one is stopping Blay and Qhuinn's love but Qhuinn. Maybe it's because Blay is such a sweetheart and a male of worth and I feel protective of him but I have a hard time forgiving Qhuinn for the pain he caused Blay. Just because he was too much of a coward to go for what he wanted. Qhuinn's loss just sayin'! Lover Unleashed was a good read but not one of my favorites in the series. <br><br><b>"What you doing out here, girlie?" the bigger of the two asked. "All alone." I'm about to cut your throat open with what I have behind my back. After which I shall break both of your legs, not because I have to, but because I shall enjoy the sound. And then I will locate something steel with which to pierce your empty chest cavity and send you back to your maker. Or mayhap I'll leave you to writhe on the ground.-Lesser and Payne</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="304618721229432183" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_157415280" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/157415280" />
    <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish"><img alt="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1398981306p2/1113032.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/157415280?book_show_action=true">Mar 29, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="user" itemprop="url" name="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish">UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=format-hard-cover">format-hard-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=series-black-dagger-brotherhood-war">series-black-dagger-brotherhood-war</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=horses-horse-racing">horses-horse-racing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=own-have-read">own-have-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=2011-reads">2011-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=mind-candy">mind-candy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=format-kindle-or-kindle-compatible">format-kindle-or-kindle-compatible</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=5-stars-or-higher">5-stars-or-higher</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=reviewed-by-me">reviewed-by-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=author-jr-ward-jessica-bird">author-jr-ward-jessica-bird</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer157415280" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1444732956785466836"><br/>This book is just all kinds of amazing!<br/><br/>**Fear thee not, spoilers are hidden**<br/><br/>There are so many things to love about <i>Lover Unleashed,</i> the 9th installment of the Black Dagger Brotherhood series. I’ve come to expect truly great stories with complex characters and lots of emotion, and this book didn’t disappoint. In fact, it ranks right up there with my favorite book in the series, Lover Awakened.<br/><br/>What makes this so amazing, you ask? Well, important things were resolved, new things were revealed and </span>
  <span id="freeText1444732956785466836" style="display:none"><br />This book is just all kinds of amazing!<br /><br />**Fear thee not, spoilers are hidden**<br /><br />There are so many things to love about <i>Lover Unleashed,</i> the 9th installment of the Black Dagger Brotherhood series. I’ve come to expect truly great stories with complex characters and lots of emotion, and this book didn’t disappoint. In fact, it ranks right up there with my favorite book in the series, Lover Awakened.<br /><br />What makes this so amazing, you ask? Well, important things were resolved, new things were revealed and with the laying of the foundation for future books complete, I can tell it’s going to be an exciting ride.<br /><br />I loved the introduction of the new warriors from England, AKA the Band of Bastards, and how they each have not just different personalities, but totally different intensities. I can see such potential for them all, but I’m wondering about the three cousins. We were given the names Xcor, Throe and Zypher, but others were only referred to as the three cousins. Those are the things that make me go, <i>hmmmmm…..</i> <br /><br />And the WARDen has such a way with words. There were many times I was laughing out loud and smiling. These are a couple of those times - <br /><br /><blockquote><i>Undeterred by his lack of enthusiasm, she leaned forward, flashing him a set of breasts that didn't so much as defy gravity as flip it off, insult its mother, and piss on it's shoes.</i><br /><br />And - <br /><br /><i>Manuel bared his teeth as if he had fangs... and did not that just turn her on.</i></blockquote><br />For those who have read the book, here are some of my more specific thoughts and comments - <br /><br /><b>Manny and Payne spoiler - </b><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I’m so glad that Manny isn’t changing! It might come to pass in another book, but it wasn’t necessary in this one and so I’m glad the issue wasn’t forced. I’m also thrilled that he’ll be able to see his mother and move between worlds, rather than having to decide on one or the other. I think it kind of opens the door for more interaction with humans, and gives the Brotherhood another connection with the outside world. <br /><br />Now, I’ve seen some criticism over Payne’s confrontation with Xcor. Some people think it was anticlimactic, but I’d have to disagree. I think that as readers of this series, we’ve become very used to the idea of a Brother coming to the rescue and saving the day and so when that doesn’t happen, or that kind of intense “rescue” doesn’t go down, it might seem rather “meh” to some readers. Personally, I thought that was handled very well! Payne showed what kind power she wields and got Xcor’s attention. That one scene gave him a lot of information in a short amount of time. I think it was done very well, indeed. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br /><br /><b>Butch and V spoiler - </b><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I have to say that my respect and admiration for Butch went through the roof in this story. What a tough spot he was in when V needed his help. He knew exactly what V needed to go through, and knew how to do it. That’s more than just friendship there. I truly believe it was their destiny to know one another. Wow… that was an amazing scene and I’ll be honest, I’m glad there was nothing sexual about it, because had it become such, I just wouldn’t have been able to continue to respect or believe in Butch and Marissa’s and Vishous and Jane’s <i>happily ever afters.</i>  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Qhuinn and Blay spoiler - </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ While we didn’t get a lot of page time here, and virtually zero interaction between the two of them, I’m thrilled at what we did get. Qhuinn finally, <i>finally</i> gets it and is moving in the right direction. I know a lot of people want them doing the horizontal mambo right now, but Qhuinn has a lot to work out before he can tackle the kind of relationship Blay deserves. Poor guy – the number his family and society have done on his head… yeah, he’s got some things to work out, for sure. And wow! What about that vision he had of the little girl with the different colored eyes… I can’t wait for all that to play out!<br /><br />I'm sorry that Qhuinn and Blay are going through so much pain right now, but I'm glad Blay has Saxton to lean on. I'm glad he's not pining away for Qhuinn, who has made it clear that a relationship for them is a no-go.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Layla spoiler - </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Wow… I’m so glad that she’s getting it together. She has such great potential as a female of worth and I loved her whole attitude in this book when talking to Qhuinn about her own feelings and how she felt about him being in love with Blay. In the past she’s come across as so needy and wimpy, and while I always knew the WARDen would show us a different side to her, I’m glad she began that process in this book! Go Layla!!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Testing the sexual waters spoiler</b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Well, I have to say that the threesome we knew to expect, while not with WHO we expected, was none-the-less quite a change from the level of sexual intensity and explicitness than we've gotten in previous books. And doesn't that just make me smile! I loved that part of the story and felt it was really well done. I can't help but think the WARDen is testing the sexuality waters for future books, and especially for Qhuinn and Blay. Two thumbs up!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Overall, I loved this book. The WARDen truly outdid herself this time and addressed so many of the things we’ve all been speculating about for years. I love the answers we got, the new question to ponder and the addition of the Band of Bastards to obsess over! Fantastic job, WARDen!!!!!! <br /><br /><br />Edited to add: And we've just learned that Tohr's book is next and is titled Lover Reborn!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1444732956785466836" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer341772882" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18025035592682937640"><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379704i/736039.jpg' alt='Image Hosted by ImageShack.us' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"You're the one who's Payne's."<br/>No hesitation on that. No hesitation on his reply either: "Yeah. I am."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><br/><b>This was such a romantic book, I must say I loved Manny and Payne's story <3 <br/>What made it even better was a side-story concerning Vishous! Fantastic :))<br/>The new bad guys are irritating as hell and I had the same urge to skip them as I do the lessers :(<br/>But overall, I loved this one <3 </b><br/><br/><br/><br/><b>The story</b><br/><br/><br/>This one picks up right after Lover Mine.<br/>Payne is at the Brotherhood compound, injured and fr</span>
  <span id="freeText18025035592682937640" style="display:none"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379704i/736039.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"You're the one who's Payne's."<br>No hesitation on that. No hesitation on his reply either: "Yeah. I am."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><b>This was such a romantic book, I must say I loved Manny and Payne's story &lt;3 <br>What made it even better was a side-story concerning Vishous! Fantastic :))<br>The new bad guys are irritating as hell and I had the same urge to skip them as I do the lessers :(<br>But overall, I loved this one &lt;3 </b><br><br><br><br><b>The story</b><br><br><br>This one picks up right after Lover Mine.<br>Payne is at the Brotherhood compound, injured and frustrated, while everyone is in shock by learning she is Vishous' sister.<br>Jane takes off to find someone who can heal Payne, her former boss and friend, Manuel Manello.<br>Manuel is shocked and angry to find out Jane is alive, but he agrees to go with her and try to help the injured person.<br>The moment he sees Payne, he knows she's special, and that she's meant to be his.<br>He operates on her, and they delete his memory after it's done, which causes Manny massive headaches and the poor guy ends up thinking he's losing his mind.<br>Payne's state isn't improving, and she doesn't want to be immobile for the rest of her life, so Vishous decides to do something to give her the will to live.<br>He brings her back her healer.<br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Lifting her palm, she peeled back and slapped him across the face. "And do NOT insult my blood."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><b>*This is Payne and Xcor quote. I just had to. It made my day :D*</b><br><br><br><br><b>The story</b> - I just LOVED the romance in this one!!! I know it isn't a favorite for most people, but for me it totally worked :) <br>And what's weird, I am really not a fan of insta-love, and this one is as insta as it gets, but yeah, it didn't bother me at all :)<br>The side-story about Vishous was heartbreaking, but I loved it as well. <br><br><b>The characters</b><br><b>Vishous</b> - He is dealing with another shock, learning he had a sister imprisoned by his mother, and it isn't doing him any good on the mental level. Payne asks him to kill her if the treatment doesn't work, and it eating him alive. He goes back to his masochistic ways, and Jane doesn't know how to help him. After Payne tries to <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[kill herself <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, he just snaps.<br><b>Vishous/Jane</b> - All is not well with these too and they go through some rocky times here. I felt terrible for both of them, but it was still good to see their relationship progress even further :)<br><b>Vishous/Butch</b> - Highlight of the book &lt;3 Loved the scenes between them, and it just shows how special their friendship (love) is. <br><b>The Band of Bastards</b> - New bad guys. Incredibly irritating. i think I liked Lash better then these guys, and that's saying something cause I hated Lash's guts completely!<br>Anyway. Maybe it's just me. But I had an incredible urge to just skip everything involving them and pretend they don't exist :)<br><b>Xcor</b> - *pukes*<br>I don't want to read about him. I don't want to know about anything concerning him. I don't want him to have his own book because that would mean I'd have to read about him a hell of a lot more than now. I don't think my brain would be able to take it.<br>But I will have to. And I will hate Ward for forcing me to read about a guy I don't want to read.<br><br><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379704i/736040.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Payne looked back through the glass at the human on the bed. "Yes. I am in love with him. And if you try to dissuade me by the fact that I have not lived yet enough to judge, I say unto you... fuck off. I need not know the world to realize my heart's desire."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br>Payne is the daughter of the Scribe Virgin, twin sister of Vishous.<br>She has been imprisoned by her mother for 300 years, because Payne had killed the Bloodletter for what he had done to Vishous.<br>Frustrated because of her imprisonment, she took it all on Wrath in the middle of their sparring sessions, which resulted in Payne getting hurt and taken out of the Sanctuary to the Brotherhood mansion, to be treated.<br>She is captivated by Manny, and doesn't want to part from him, even though she knows she must erase his memories after he's done treating her.<br>When the operation succeeds, but she remains immobile, Payne loses the will to live.<br>Seeing Manny is the thing that brings her back, and he shows her there's more to life even when one can't walk.<br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I want you..." Reaching for the bottom of his loose shirt, he pulled it up slowly, exposing the carved muscles of his stomach. "…to want me."<br>Oh, sweet destiny, she did.<br>And he meant what he said. The more she looked, the more those abdominals of his curled and released as if he were breathing hard as well.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br>She is a fighter, strong and capable, and being without her legs is killing her. Manny is the only thing that makes her want to live, and they realise her feelings for him are the thing that could make her better :)<br>Well, I really liked her as a character :) She's pretty much clueless as to relationships, but she isn't stupid. She realises she feels something for Manny, and the more they spend time together, the more she falls in love with him.<br>The scene with the horse was very sweet &lt;3 <br>And when she kicks ass in front of his car LMAO :D awesome scene :)<br>But my favorite didn't include Manny with her, it was Payne and Xcor! <br>How she behaved with him! <br>*bows*<br>The slap! I loved her at that moment, I really did. I wanted to slap him too. And maybe kick him in the balls or something. Oh well :)<br><br><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380805955i/3123895.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"This meant he was a movie star, a drill sergeant, and the president of the United States all rolled up into a sixfoot-tall, stacked son of a bitch. He had a terrible temper, a stunning intellect, and a fuse that was about a millimeter long.<br>On a good day."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br>Manny is overbearing, used to giving orders and having a short leash on his temper.<br>He had feelings for his friend and colleague, Jane, and after she dies, he was completely crushed.<br>Now he sees her again, and is beyond angry at her for lying to him, but still accepts to treat the patient that's in dire need of his help.<br>When he sees Payne, he knows she is HIS, even though it doesn't make sense to him at all. He is very territorial, and has the urge to do the best he can to help her.<br>After the surgery, his memory is deleted and he thinks he's going crazy, until Vishous approaches him and asks for his help again.<br>Payne doesn't want to live that way, and Manny shows her it isn't that bad, and their mutual attraction is the thing that will get them together, and make Payne better :)<br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"How old are you?" he asked abruptly. He might be a letch, but he didn't do underage anything. She was sure as hell built like an adult, but who knew what their maturity rate was—"<br>I am three hundred and five years of age."<br>Blink. Blink. Annnnnnd one more for good measure. Sure as shit that had to be of age, he thought.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br>He's very funny, I loved his thoughts and POV :))))<br>Even though he's a mere human, he isn't intimidated by V who absolutely hates his guts, and threatens to kill him :DDDDD<br>He wants Payne, but knows he can't have her, even after he gets his memories back.<br>He does want to help her heal, so he decides to stay for however long it takes for her to get better :)<br>All the scenes between Vishous and Manny were hilarious :D loved them both and how neither of them backed down :D<br>When he took her exploring around town, that was sweet, and the scene with his horse too...<br>The first goodbye in the hospital... Awesome scene!!! I felt so bad for him!<br>And the scene in his bedroom when she came with good news :((((<br>Heartbreaking!<br>The end was wonderful and I seriously can't wait to see more of Manny and Payne in the next books. Love them both!!!!!<br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"All his life he'd wondered why he'd never fallen in love, and now he knew: He'd been waiting for this moment, this woman, this time.<br>The female is mine, he thought.<br>And even though that made no sense at all, the conviction was so strong, he couldn't question it."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><br><br><br><b>My favorite quotes from other characters:</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379704i/736041.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379704i/736042.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"She's your sister?"<br>"Don't forget it."<br>Manny smiled by baring all his teeth. "Then there's something you need to know."<br>"What."<br>Manny rose up on his toes and met the fucker eye-to-eye. "If you think you want to kill me now, this ain't nothin' compared to how you're going to feel when I see her again."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379704i/736041.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379704i/736043.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I would do anything for you. Anything."<br>With that, he pushed his way out... and as the door eased shut, she realized that I love you could indeed be said without actually uttering the phrase.<br>Actions did mean more than words.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379704i/736041.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379704i/736044.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>V stepped in close, bringing their faces to within an inch of each other. "You don't have the stomach for it. Trust me."<br>Those deep hazel eyes held his and didn't blink. "You'd be amazed what I would do to keep you alive."<br>Abruptly, V's mouth opened, his breath growing tight. And as the two of them stood chest-tochest, he knew every inch of his body, felt all of it at once.<br>"What are you saying, cop."<br>-----------------------------------------------<br>There should be something said between them, V thought. There was just so much...<br>to be said.<br>"I want it from you," V bit out. "I need it."<br>Butch nodded. "I know."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379704i/736041.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379704i/736045.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Vishous rolled them over, keeping them joined, and his eyes roamed her face for a long moment. "I have no words. Sixteen languages, but no words."<br>There was both love and despair in his voice. He was truly handicapped when it came to emotions, and falling in love hadn't changed that... at least, not when things were as stressful as they were right now. But that was okay—after this time together it was okay.<br>---------------------------------------<br>"Yes?" he drawled. When she seemed speechless, he sucked on her lip and growled, "If you recall, we were discussing the bathroom? I was thinking maybe I could reacquaint the pair of you. Not sure if you're aware of it, but that sink counter has been crying out for you."<br>"And you do some of your best work at sinks."<br>V dragged one fang up her throat. "True that."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379704i/736041.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Jesus Christ... to be three hundred years old and find out you had a sibling.<br>Nice move, moms. Real fucking nice.<br>To think he'd assumed he'd worked through all of his issues with his parents.<br>Then again, only one of them was dead. If the Scribe Virgin would just go the way of the Bloodletter and kick it, maybe he'd manage to get on an even keel."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379704i/736046.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Christ, he so didn't need a mirror to see himself for the coward and the fraud he was... but there was nothing he could do about it. He was locked in a cage with no key that he could find, years of his family's derision boxing him in and cramping him: The truth behind his wild side was that he was a straight-up pussy. Blay, on the other hand, was the strong one. Tired of waiting around, he'd declared who he was and found somebody to be with."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><br><br><br><b>Lots of quotes by Vishous, but I just couldn't help it :)<br>I love him &lt;3</b><br><br><br><br><br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_118760126" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/118760126" />
    <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1352609417p2/2489554.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/118760126?book_show_action=true">Aug 26, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog">Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">BDB fans and paranormal romance fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-i-go-rabid-over">books-i-go-rabid-over</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=covers-to-covet">covers-to-covet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=read-in-2011">read-in-2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-i-own">books-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=signed-by-author">signed-by-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=bondage">bondage</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=king-of-the-harem">king-of-the-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=drinks-on-me">drinks-on-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=my-hottie-harem">my-hottie-harem</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer118760126" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15048265886409041433">Reading about the Black Dagger Brotherhood is like catching up with old friends. I can’t express how much I love this entire series! It’s #1 in my eyes and will forever stay that way!<br/><br/><i> Lover Unleashed</i> is Payne and Manny’s book and although I would have liked to see more romance between the two, I found that I really enjoyed both of them! <b>Manny</b> wasn’t exactly my favourite character in <i> Lover Unbound</i> only because he was competition for V, but I found myself falling for the hot doctor. He had big sh</span>
  <span id="freeText15048265886409041433" style="display:none">Reading about the Black Dagger Brotherhood is like catching up with old friends. I can’t express how much I love this entire series! It’s #1 in my eyes and will forever stay that way!<br><br><i> Lover Unleashed</i> is Payne and Manny’s book and although I would have liked to see more romance between the two, I found that I really enjoyed both of them! <b>Manny</b> wasn’t exactly my favourite character in <i> Lover Unbound</i> only because he was competition for V, but I found myself falling for the hot doctor. He had big shoes to fill if he wanted to roll with the Brothers and I thought he handled himself well. I loved his toughness and arrogant demeanour in the OR room and his gentleness with Payne. He’s also got a bit of a smart mouth, and you know I just can’t resist that! I’ll be your bambina any day, babe!<br><br><b>Payne</b> was awesome. I love the way she talks! There’s something about her that makes her seem innocent and yet not, if that makes any sense at all. And even injured and unmoving, she’s still a potent force in this book. My heart broke for her when she yelled at V for snatching away her one chance at escape. Going from her mother’s imprisonment to being a prisoner in her own body, I can understand her wish for a way out. But it still broke my heart to see it.<br><br>Then there’s <b>V</b> who seriously goes batshit crazy in this one. After hearing he had a twin sister after all these years, he’s seriously pissed off with Mommy Dearest right now and I don’t blame him. He hasn’t ever had a stable relationship with her so when this bomb dropped, I could understand why he had a WTF reaction. <br><br>What I love about this series is the fact that J.R. doesn’t sugar coat her relationships. There are ups and downs within each of the Brother’s relationships, just like any other relationships. I feel that the troubles V and Jane face strengthen their bond more than if they were just happy-happy-merry-merry all the time. In fact, having not been completely taken away by the romance in <i> Lover Unbound</i>, I felt that this book really solidified the fact that V and Jane were meant to be together. I didn’t feel it back in V’s book, but after nearly breaking everything off in this one and making amends, it works in bringing back the romance. <br><br>I liked that J.R. explored the lows in their relationship but I also thought that V’s drama stole some of the spotlight from Payne and Manny. Sometimes the balance between Manny/Payne and V/Jane were conflicting and I would have liked to see more of a focus on Manuelo and my girl, Payne. After all, it is their book!<br><br><b> Jane</b> was my least favourite <i>shellan</i> but reading about her conflicted feelings, I grew into her more. I always saw her as this unemotional, callous one, but seeing her panic and fear at watching V stumble in injured made me realize how much she cared. And it was enough for me. <br><br>Ward covers a lot of bases in this one. <b>Xcor</b> (is it pronounced Cor?) and his band of bastards are introduced and I was VERY excited to read about new characters. I can see a whole new world that she can explore with these men and I really enjoyed the prologue. It was badass! And that scene with Xcor, Throe and that chick? Wow.<br><br>Then there’s <b>Qhuinn</b> who is still suffering from a shattered heart. With John dealing with mated life and Blay off with Sax, Qhuinn is having to deal with things on his own when he should be with his boys. I felt so bad for him. WHEN IS HIS BOOK COMING OUT!? This guy deserves a HEA the most!!<br><br>I loved this book and even though it wasn’t my favourite of the series, I can still say that I loved to read about Manny and Payne! The shit with V and Jane helped fixed the mediocre romance in <i>Lover Unbound</i> and <b>QHUINN AND BLAY NEED THEIR DAMN BOOK ALREADY!!</b> What’s a chick gotta do to get her M/M lovin? <br><br>Here’s my <b>Payne</b><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>And this is my <b>Manny</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379750227i/126204._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="15048265886409041433" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_884887836" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/884887836" />
    <a title="P " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25327841-p"><img alt="P " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1489853536p2/25327841.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/884887836?book_show_action=true">Mar 18, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="P " class="user" itemprop="url" name="P " href="/user/show/25327841-p">P </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25327841-p?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer884887836" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer965503336834509852"><b>
  <blockquote>“With that, he pushed his way out...and as the door eased shut, she realized I love you could indeed be said without actually uttering the phrase. Actions did mean more than words.”</blockquote>
</b> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479486475i/21196845.jpg' width='400' height='430' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>To be honest, I really don't know why I gave this book 5 stars as for my distaste for the start. Payne is not a likable heroine for me, she's just too masculine and indepedent that I didn't know how Ward could find a man to match her with. And finally she fould Manny, yes it's him Dr. Manuel Manello, the Handsome</span>
  <span id="freeText965503336834509852" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>“With that, he pushed his way out...and as the door eased shut, she realized I love you could indeed be said without actually uttering the phrase. Actions did mean more than words.”</blockquote>
</b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479486475i/21196845.jpg" width="400" height="430" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To be honest, I really don't know why I gave this book 5 stars as for my distaste for the start. Payne is not a likable heroine for me, she's just too masculine and indepedent that I didn't know how Ward could find a man to match her with. And finally she fould Manny, yes it's him Dr. Manuel Manello, the Handsome one who had a crush on Dr.Jane since V's book. I wasn't so sure that the chemistry between them could convince me to believe that they are the hero and heroine of this book and destined to be together after all. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1479486475ra/21196846.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“Butch tightened his grip on his cell and wished there were an app that let you reach through a phone and bitch slap someone.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br>BUT J.R. Ward proved me wrong again because her story was woven in the discreet resonant from the start, I was astounded by the connection she linked from one character to another flawlessly and knew that this was what she was good at. Manny is a normal man, yet he has the guts. While Payne seems to be independent, she is still innocent and looking for Manny's attention when she's with him.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“I came to you, Jane. Every night this week, I came to you. I didn't want you to be alone. And I didn't want to sleep without you."</blockquote>
</b><br><br>The ending fucked my mind. OMFG ! that was nothing I'd expected before. The revelation is everything. Although this is not the best book of the series, but it's unputdownable because of the narration and twists. V and Jane's story is very interesting and I was glad that we see them again in this book.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1479486475ra/21196847.gif" width="400" height="160" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://goo.gl/d2V2rd">https://goo.gl/d2V2rd</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="965503336834509852" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer4142052598931182916">WOW! <b>
  <i>Lover Unleashed</i>
</b> is a fantastic installment to the <i>Black Dagger Brotherhood</i>, and I especially loved the romance this time! <br/><br/>Here’s a checklist rundown of some of my favorite highpoints:<br/><br/>*More romance between main H/H? – Check!<blockquote>Manny and Payne were amazing characters, and I absolutely loved, <i>loved, luvvved</i> them together! They were such a sweet, sexy couple with a strong emotional connection and explosive chemistry. In fact, their sensual, evocative romance was possibly my favorite since <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/35729.Lover_Eternal__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___2_' title='Lover Eternal (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #2) by J.R. Ward' rel='nofollow noopener'>Love</a></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText4142052598931182916" style="display:none">WOW! <b>
  <i>Lover Unleashed</i>
</b> is a fantastic installment to the <i>Black Dagger Brotherhood</i>, and I especially loved the romance this time! <br /><br />Here’s a checklist rundown of some of my favorite highpoints:<br /><br />*More romance between main H/H? – Check!<blockquote>Manny and Payne were amazing characters, and I absolutely loved, <i>loved, luvvved</i> them together! They were such a sweet, sexy couple with a strong emotional connection and explosive chemistry. In fact, their sensual, evocative romance was possibly my favorite since <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/35729.Lover_Eternal__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___2_" title="Lover Eternal (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #2) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Eternal</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/42900.Lover_Awakened__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___3_" title="Lover Awakened (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #3) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Awakened</a>.</blockquote><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[

  <blockquote>I loved that this also provided closure for doors cracked but never fully opened between V and Butch. As agonizing as it was for Butch to help V break down his emotional and psychological walls, their intrinsic bond of friendship was never more necessary. And I’m glad it was done without crossing any sexual lines between them because that would have completely nullified the hard-fought HEAs between V/Jane and Butch/Marissa.</blockquote>

Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Envy</a> comes out!</blockquote><br />*Qhuinn being less of a manwhore and finally getting his shit together? – Not quite a check, but he’s making some progress...at least it looks promising.<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[*Hot Qhuay lovin’? – DENIED! I’m optimistic that things are finally headed in the right direction, though. But I don’t want Layla in the mix, at all! True?</blockquote> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>	<br /><br />There were a few things that could have been better.<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[*The <i>finally!</i> love scene between Manny and Payne was much too brief and not nearly as detailed or hot as I was hoping for, especially after so much buildup.<br />*I wanted a mating ceremony between V/Jane and Manny/Payne. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br />*The ending was too abrupt and it needed an epilogue, especially since we have to wait another year until the next book!<br /><br />Overall, this is a terrific read and one of the better, more satisfying additions to the phenomenal BDB series. 5 stars!<br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_154781667" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/154781667" />
    <a title="Mandi Schreiner" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2704703-mandi-schreiner"><img alt="Mandi Schreiner" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1368979996p2/2704703.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/154781667?book_show_action=true">Mar 16, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mandi Schreiner" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mandi Schreiner" href="/user/show/2704703-mandi-schreiner">Mandi Schreiner</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer154781667&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer154781667" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16009195703805821099">Lover Unleashed, book nine in my beloved Black Dagger Brotherhood series is Manny and Payne’s book – or so we were told. But honestly, this book is Vishous’s. True? Vishous steals the show. Manny and Payne have a romance, but their story is nothing compared to V’s. Nothing. There is also no way this one can be read as a stand alone – you need V’s backstory throughout the entire series to get anything from this book.<br/><br/>I was definitely disappointed with the ending of V’s book Lover Unbound, when Jan</span>
  <span id="freeText16009195703805821099" style="display:none">Lover Unleashed, book nine in my beloved Black Dagger Brotherhood series is Manny and Payne’s book – or so we were told. But honestly, this book is Vishous’s. True? Vishous steals the show. Manny and Payne have a romance, but their story is nothing compared to V’s. Nothing. There is also no way this one can be read as a stand alone – you need V’s backstory throughout the entire series to get anything from this book.<br /><br />I was definitely disappointed with the ending of V’s book Lover Unbound, when Jane was turned into a ghost. Not only with the ghost aspect, but I just wanted more of a closure with V and Jane but we get it in this book. V is not in a good place. Payne comes to his side, paralyzed from a sparring session with Wrath. Vishous has had no idea in the 300 years he has been alive that he even had a twin sister. The Scribe Virgin, their mother (who is not in this book which is a shame), has had Payne imprisoned. Now she is here, in his life, and the protectiveness V feels for her is out of control.<br /><br />When Jane calls Manny in to help operate on her, there is that instant “mine” between them (even though Manny is a human). This does not go over well with V, as Butch and the other brothers struggle to keep him from killing Manny. As time goes on, V goes into an even deeper downward spiral. Payne doesn’t heal as she should, and when Jane attempts something shocking, he walks away – from Jane. This scene is very moving and well done. What we really get is V coming to terms with his abusive father, his negligent mother, and his role as a hellren. Yes he loves Jane, but can he overcome his past, and his current broken self to give her what she needs? Can he fulfill the new role as a brother to Payne?<br /><br />Butch plays a very important role in “saving” V. I won’t go into specifics as to not spoil too much, but this issue had to be addressed. He is in love with Butch as we all know. We finally get a little more exploration into this relationship - the one we were teased with in Lover Unbound.<br /><br />As the other continued fighting, the pair of them just stared at each other against the audio backdrop of grunts and metal-to-metal strikes and inventive cursing. There should be something said between them, V thought. There was just so much…to be said.<br /><br />“I want it from you,” V bit out. “I need it.”<br /><br />Butch nodded. “I know.”<br /><br /> <br /><br />And just to note – the “it” is not exactly what you think. Also *Mandi dies*<br /><br />Before I started the book I thought how in the world will anything happen between V and Butch with both of them mated (to Jane and Marissa). But it works out totally fine. And it is not the actual scene that fulfilled me, but a scene with them later – a very quiet peaceful moment that to me, lets me breathe a sigh of contentment for these two males. I still don’t know if JR Ward gives Butch and V a fair shot – the big scene with V and Butch is kind of short. But I’m glad she does what she does.<br /><br />And I have to say, I actually liked Jane in this book – crazy, right? I think JR Ward does a nice job with the emotional turmoil between these two. There is one scene where V just walks away from her – and it is heartbreaking. But I get her more. I understand her more. I like her with V now. I’m content with their relationship. And we get several dirty sex scenes with them:<br /><br />“Vishous…”<br /><br />“What”<br /><br />His gloved hand dipped under the black satin, and she didn’t have to see where it went to be well aware he’d gripped himself. The fact that he arched back told her everything she needed to know. That and the way he bit down on his lower lip.<br /><br />“Jane…”<br /><br />“What.”<br /><br />“Are you just going to watch, true?”<br /><br />We also get some classic V and Butch moments that make me smile:<br /><br />Butch clapped him on the shoulder. “Listen to me. You have the fashion sense of a park bench and the interpersonal skills of a meat cleaver – “<br /><br />“Is this suppose to be helping?”<br /><br />“Let me finish-“<br /><br />“What’s next? The size of my cock?”<br /><br />“Hey, even pencils can get the job done – I’ve heard the moaning from your room to prove it.”<br /><br />Let’s move onto Blay and Qhuinn, or as they are called “Qhuay.” They had such a presence in Lover Mine I am disappointed with the lack of progress in their relationship. I hear a novella might be in the works for them so maybe JR Ward is saving up for that – but still, there is no Qhuay in this book. We get a tiny bit with Blay and Saxton. And we get a little more than that with Qhuinn and Layla (OMG – I can’t even go there right now). We get a big reveal with Qhuinn – something that will happen in the future. We need to discuss this my friends….soon.<br /><br />No Lassiter or Tohr in this one. No Murhder, which surprised me since we were introduced to him in Lover Mine. There is also an odd side story of a serial murderer. Now in it, we are introduced to Jose de la Cruz’s new partner Thomas DelVecchio Jr, or Veck. I can only hope Veck plays some kind of role in the next book because otherwise I have no idea why this storyline is in it. Unless I missed something. Veck does have some strange…ways, so I assume there is more to come of him. I’m very intrigued.<br /><br />We meet some new vampires, not necessarily brothers, but six men (although we really only meet three) that fight lessors. They fought under the Bloodletter until he died, and the Xcor took over. Along with Throe and Zypher, they are a secret band of “brothers” – I use that term loosely because they are not necessarily like The Brothers. They fight together –killing lessors, or humans. They are much more violent without as many morals. They have been living in the old country, but have realized, most of the lessors have moved to where the Brotherhood now reside. Xcor wants one thing – to be king. So they move near Caldwell and start to set things in motion. So, yes they fight lessors, but they are not necessarily friendly with the brotherhood. I am interested to see how this plays out. The brotherhood is aware of Xcor, but we don’t get any details of the how or why. It looks like the new conflict might be moving away from the lessors and more towards a fight with Xcor for the King.<br /><br />I suppose I can’t leave Payne and Manny out. Honestly, they did nothing for me. If I had to hear Payne say “Verily” one more time I might have thrown the book. For some reason I thought Payne was going to be similar to Xhex, but she ends up more like Layla. She has a few kick ass moments towards the end but I didn’t feel like she was a warrior or a brother like Xhex is. There was just nothing that stood out about them. I like Manny – he had nice interactions with Jane. And I liked out he stood up to Vishous and his interactions with Butch are fun. But for the actual romance between these two – it did nothing for me, which makes it really hard to rate this book. Also – the way Payne ends up healing is so corny. I’m sorry – but I just didn’t get it.<br /><br />While Lover Mine really took us back to the romance, away from the UF feel after book 3, this one takes us right back. In a way, I don’t want to complain because the spotlight is on Vishous. And I LOVE Vishous. Before I started this book, my one hope was that we got a lot of Vishous material. Little did I know he would be the entire book. He even announces at the end that he is officially mating with Jane (tattoo on his back etc). Seriously, this is his book.<br /><br />Bottom line is – I have very mixed feelings. The book entertained me. I read it in one day. I love this series, I love the brothers, I really enjoy JR Ward’s style of writing. I love that we get tons of stuff with Vishous. I think Vishous’s story needed to be continued, but it was at the expense of the main characters. Honestly, I wasn’t invested at all in Payne and Manny, so not getting a full story from them isn’t all that heartbreaking to me. But – this is their book. And they get jipped. With the lack of Blay and Qhuinn after such a build-up in the previous book, I can’t help but be a little disappointed.<br /><br />I also want to note that no one is really set up to be next in the series – and that is driving me crazy!!! I’m very curious to see who it is!!!!<br /><br />Rating: C+ maybe a B-</span>
  <a data-text-id="16009195703805821099" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
