<div id="review_99964660" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/99964660" />
    <a title="Buggy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3099666-buggy"><img alt="Buggy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1289702969p2/3099666.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/99964660?book_show_action=true">Apr 24, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Buggy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Buggy" href="/user/show/3099666-buggy">Buggy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3099666-buggy?shelf=paranormal-rom">paranormal-rom</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3099666-buggy?shelf=urb-fantasy">urb-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3099666-buggy?shelf=top">top</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3099666-buggy?shelf=shelf-12">shelf-12</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3099666-buggy?shelf=tortured-hero">tortured-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3099666-buggy?shelf=tie-me-up">tie-me-up</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3099666-buggy?shelf=scars-r-sexy">scars-r-sexy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3099666-buggy?shelf=re-read">re-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3099666-buggy?shelf=ghosts">ghosts</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3099666-buggy?shelf=vampalicious">vampalicious</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer99964660" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14885575507512587180">Opening Line: <i>"Xcor saw his father killed when he was but five years past his transition."</i><br/><b>**Spoiler Free**</b><br/>Ah yes, how sweet it is to be back with the Black Dagger Brotherhood. It was with some anticipation (understatement) that I cracked open the 489 pages I’d waited almost a year on, and it was with baited breathe that I began. Wondering exactly what direction JR Ward was going to take this 9th instalment in? Well I can tell you that with this one she does not disappoint, giving us fans exactly</span>
  <span id="freeText14885575507512587180" style="display:none">Opening Line: <i>"Xcor saw his father killed when he was but five years past his transition."</i><br /><b>**Spoiler Free**</b><br />Ah yes, how sweet it is to be back with the Black Dagger Brotherhood. It was with some anticipation (understatement) that I cracked open the 489 pages I’d waited almost a year on, and it was with baited breathe that I began. Wondering exactly what direction JR Ward was going to take this 9th instalment in? Well I can tell you that with this one she does not disappoint, giving us fans exactly what we've been waiting for and then some. <br /><br />Starting where (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7046495.Lover_Mine__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___8_" title="Lover Mine (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #8) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Mine</a>) left off and with her usual flair (the first 4 words will have you smiling) we get; multiple POV’s, evolving story lines, ass-kicking action and major injuries to most of the Brotherhood. We revisit past characters(Jose del la Cruz) while being introduced to new ones, including (among others) the intriguing ‘Band of Bastards’. This group of 6 is around to stay and with them comes an endless supply of future story possibilities. <br /><br />With blasts of tension, humour, romance and way erotic love scenes we witness a couple of characters fall apart, see unrequited love, get major hints of things to come, and while laughing with Rhage and Fritz in the billiards room we also worry about the future of the King. Even though our main love story here is not as dominant as in past books, I have no complaints as Ward manages to include and give us moments with each and every member of the Brotherhood mansion in one way or another. And while I ached for Qhuinn and Blay, then there was V. And oh the V. True? <br /><br />As much as this is pegged as Payne and Manny’s book LOVER UNLEASHED really belongs to Vishous and isn't it great (understatement) to be back in his, intricate, messed up, dirty lil mind. Along with Butch and Jane this trio goes to some very dark places, taking us right along for the excruciating ride and finally putting to bed (so to speak) Butch and V’s relationship once and for all. I loved revisiting V and through him, hearing from the Cop again as well as getting to know Jane better-who has at last stopped feeling like a ghost (I may forgive Ward yet for killing her) And in the afterward, those quiet moments spent between Butch and V well … in his words, <i>“I have no words. Sixteen languages, but no words.”</i><br /><br />All this awesomeness has of course been wrapped up with Ward's unique style of writing although this time there's a different vibe to it and it took me a while to put my finger on what it was. The multiple f-bombs, rap references and Wardisms are still here but she's managed to stop jumping around as we did in LOVER MINE with Ghostbuster storylines and Old Country flashbacks.<br /><br />She's also toned down the product placement and riddle filled sentences ((i.e.<i>“A gust of wind went Nike across the flat landscape"</i> And with less 'Lessers' to contend with here (much like in(<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/304027.Lover_Unbound__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___5_" title="Lover Unbound (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #5) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Unbound</a>)and them operating without a visible leader's POV the entire story flows better and you don't find yourself grumbling, wanting to skip ahead. Overall this feels more like one of the original books from the series then the urban fantasy-ish instalments of late.<br /><br />Regarding Payne and Manny; I enjoyed this couple, <i>verily</i> I did. I’ve loved Manny from the first time we met him and enjoyed getting to know him here. His interactions/revelations with Butch are hilarious as is his discovery of Jane and the whole BDB world. Payne wasn’t as tough as I was expecting although she does manage to rescue herself while spending a considerable amount of time paralyzed. Manny’s method of healing her is very... Marvin Gaye and although their actual HEA is kinda corny I liked how Ward found a way to keep them together. <br /><br />In the end Ward leaves us smiling with contentment (although I had been hoping for a mating ceremony and not the one you’d expect) and with events wide open for future stories that I can't wait to discover. I just wish it wasn't so far away because after spending just a few days with the BDB I'm not ready to let them go yet. See ya next year boys, stay safe. True.<br /><br />Oh I've also just learned that book #10 will be Tohrment’s story. Wow that's bound to be a tearjerker. Cheers </span>
  <a data-text-id="14885575507512587180" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_99963488" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/99963488" />
    <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"><img alt=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1403239075p2/1570669.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/99963488?book_show_action=true">Apr 24, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="user" itemprop="url" name=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"> Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Vamp romance lovers</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=favorite-or-autobuy-author">favorite-or-autobuy-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=medical-profession">medical-profession</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=vampire">vampire</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=hero-to-die-for">hero-to-die-for</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=owned-copy">owned-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=brotherhood">brotherhood</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=2011-reading">2011-reading</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer99963488&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer99963488" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18439715760867393231">Warning: Very Long Review!<br/><br/>Let me start this review of Lover Unleashed with a letter to Manuel Manello, MD.<br/><br/><i>Dear Dr. Manny:<br/>Ah, Manny. Why did you have to go and steal my heart? You are such a darling man. Just perfect for the daughter of the Bloodletter, Payne. You even gave her a horse as an engagement present. You truly know the way to a woman’s heart. And, did I mention that you are a fantastic doctor? The Brotherhood is very fortunate to have your services. <br/>So you found a long-lost brother, an</i></span>
  <span id="freeText18439715760867393231" style="display:none">Warning: Very Long Review!<br /><br />Let me start this review of Lover Unleashed with a letter to Manuel Manello, MD.<br /><br /><i>Dear Dr. Manny:<br />Ah, Manny. Why did you have to go and steal my heart? You are such a darling man. Just perfect for the daughter of the Bloodletter, Payne. You even gave her a horse as an engagement present. You truly know the way to a woman’s heart. And, did I mention that you are a fantastic doctor? The Brotherhood is very fortunate to have your services. <br />So you found a long-lost brother, and boy do you have some things in common. Namely, you are both tough guys who are sweet as molasses down deep, and know how to take care of your women. And you’re both hot! (Clears throat and wipes glow away from brow.)<br />Anyway…<br />You really took all the vampires are real stuff in stride. And you have exquisite taste in women. You love a strong woman who can kick some serious butt, and a beautiful woman who glows (and I do mean glows) when she’s happy. It’s clear that you’d give her the blood from your veins, and all the sexual healing a woman needs. (yeah, you’re really good at that) And when you apply your doctoring skills to your patient, you really go the extra mile. <br />And then there’s the fact that you are not at all scared of a six-foot, six inches tall brother who thinks his twin sister is too young to have sex, not to mention, doesn’t think any male is good enough for her. You more than proved your worth to him and the rest of the Brotherhood, in the trenches, and otherwise.<br />Manny, Manny, Manny, can I add you to my ranks of favorite heroes, just because you are super-duper awesome? I had a feeling I would like you as the hero of your own book. Turns out I was right. Thanks for giving me such a fantastic story. I’ll have you know that your book is displayed with pride on my shelf with John Matthew and Rehvenge’s books. That’s a real honor. You deserve it.<br />I hope you will be very happy with Payne. <br />Love, hugs and kisses to you.<br /><br />Your adoring fan, <br />Danielle</i><br /><br /><b>Now Here's My Official Review!</b>:<br />Well, if you didn’t notice by reading my letter to Manny, I really loved this book. I admit I was a bit apprehensive because of some of the rumors I heard. But I was a happy camper in the end. The WARDen handled some tricky issues (for me) beautifully.<br /><br /><b>Vishous and His Relationships With Jane, Butch, and Payne</b><br />I love the intimate, intense, multi-faceted relationship between Vishous and Butch. However, I am not one of the people who think that they are a better couple than Vishous/Jane and Butch/Marissa. I think Jane is absolutely perfect for Vishous. She understands him deeply, and loves him for who he is. I loved that Jane made some tough choices out of her love for Vishous, and she never resented Vishous and Butch’s close relationship. That’s a confident, strong woman for you. The right woman for Vishous. Hi Five to Jane for being awesome!<br /><br />This book was a good chance to see deeper into the complicated world of Vishous, son of the Bloodletter. I loved Vishous in his book, and I love him even more now. He is one wounded guy. He doesn’t wear his pain on his sleeve like some heroes. Instead, he has buried most of it, and the other part comes out in his need for dark, twisted sex and in his formidable fighting skills against the Lessers. Since he found Jane, he realized that sex could be about love, and he put that (dark, painful sex) aside, although he still likes a little kink in his sex (which is okay with Jane). However, with his issues he faces in this book with finding out he had a sister that his mother kept from him, and with Payne’s injury and her despair about not getting better, he needs an outlet. How can he do that without betraying his vows to Jane? Also, why does he feel like he didn’t give all to Jane and show her exactly how much she means? Can this son of the Bloodletter, a dark soul who was completely rejected by both mother and father, really be worthy of a loving relationship, and still be true to who he is? All those issues were dealt with. At one point in this book, I was truly worried. I thought that V and Jane were going to fracture down the middle, and I really didn’t want that, because I love them together. I needn’t have worried. The WARDen came through for me. I was foolish to think she wouldn’t, for I know she loves these characters even more than I do. <br /><br />It’s really hard to put my feelings into words here. There was something so touching about the bonds that V shares with Jane and Butch. I loved that he was able to be close to Butch without betraying his marriage bond with Jane. V and Butch have a fantastic, one of a kind relationship. I was worried about what needed to happen for Vishous at Butch’s hands, but Butch knew exactly what to do. He got right to the heart of the matter, and gave Vishous the release he needed (get your mind out the gutter). <br /><br />The thing I love most about JR Ward’s writing is on evidence here. She does the interplay of emotions within and between her characters so well. She doesn’t go for the easy answer. She makes things tough for her creations, just like life is full of hard spots and crappy situations. But somehow, even though things can be bittersweet, she always gives us hope. With Vishous and Jane and Butch, I know that there is so much hope there. They will always have each other, just as Butch has Marissa (who also understands the bond between Vishous and Butch). And now, Butch and Vishous have a bond with Manny, very much about ‘brotherhood.’ In fact, this book shows that bonds of blood and friendship are what life is all about, because no man is an island. Bravo, Ms. Ward for bringing this theme to light so eloquently.<br /><b>Payne and Manny</b>:<br />I haven’t known Payne that long, and I met Manny briefly in one of the earlier books. But I liked what I saw of them as characters, and I liked the idea of them together when I heard that the WARDen had paired the two. I wasn’t sure how their relationship would play out, but I have to say that their courtship strikes me as one of the more romantic ones in this book series. There was a sweetness there, both characters star-struck by each other. To Manny, Payne is a beautiful woman not of his world, and way too good for him. He’d do anything to see her healthy and happy, even knowing he has no place in her world. To Payne, Manny is her beloved Healer. He is a gorgeous, worthy male, who has given her a new life. She doesn’t want to say goodbye to him, even though she knows he’s not of her world. Manny is such a gentleman, a hellren any female would want. Payne is a tough girl, but also elegant and beautiful, even if she doesn’t see herself that way. They both have insecurities that they have to deal with in order to find their way together, but they come to realize that love can make allowances for pretty much any shortcoming. I loved the sweetness of their relationship, but also the spicy sexuality of it. Talking about hot! Their short courtship steamed up my room as I read. I knew that there had better be a way for them to be together. Thankfully there was. I know that they are a couple that I want to see more of in the forthcoming books, but I also got to see them get their happily ever after, which was just what I wanted. <br /><br />PS. I also like Manny’s relationship with Jane. They were both isolated people, dedicated to their professions, but they found a bond with each other in their past lives. It was good to see that this bond was renewed and strengthened in this book.<br /><b>Qhuinn/Blay</b>:<br />I like Qhuinn, but he annoys the crap out of me with his slutty ways. I realize it was a tremendous defense mechanism, but it got old for me. To be honest, I was glad to see Blay move on with Saxton, and stop eating his heart out over Qhuinn, although the romantic in me wanted to see these two souls get together. However, Qhuinn needed to do some growing up, and Blay needed to live his life not weighted down by his enormous unrequited love for Qhuinn. Once again, I feel the WARDen comes through here. Although there is not yet a HEA for this couple, Qhuinn is on his way to recovery. His eyes are open now. He understands that he can’t find what he was looking for in his destructive ways. He can’t hide behind the slutty, careless, Goth, playboy image, because the truth will hit him in the face eventually. Now, he has shed this hurtful façade that made it hard for me to like him, and is ready for a real relationship. However, he is willing to put his beloved’s needs before his own. This was the breakthrough I was waiting for. Now, I am eager to see these two get together. I know their book is going to be very awesome. I liked that in this book, Blay is the one who finally has someone. I think that Saxton knows exactly what’s up, and he’s okay with what he has of Blay, for as long as he has it. At the same time, he’s not unaware or unsympathetic to Qhuinn’s feelings for Blay. Sax is a good guy. I like him. It was interesting to see that Blay is the one who’s a little bit near-sighted here. He knows he still loves Qhuinn, but he also feels strongly for Sax. He feels at peace with what he has, even though his heart still beats for Qhuinn. Things are as complicated as ever, ala JR Ward! This chapter of the Qhuinn/Blay romance was very bittersweet, but I do feel optimistic for their future…finally!<br /><b>The Advent of Xcor and the Band of Bastards</b>:<br />Okay, at first I did not like Xcor. He’s not a nice guy…at all. And yet…..I’m drawn into his story. It’s my darned weakness for dark, dangerous guys. It gets me everytime. Already feel like the dude needs a love prescription. My mind is wondering where the WARDen will take this guy. I do like Throe quite a bit. He has the gentlemanly vibe I can’t resist. His sense of honor and justice is strong, and I like that about him. He might also be Xcor’s conscience. I like the loyalty he shows. And it’s clear that Xcor values him and the rest of his crew. He demands loyalty implicitly, but he shows that he is worthy of it, in his rough way. I definitely want to see more of these guys.<br />Okay, a moment of honesty here. I admit, I don’t go for ménage in romance. It’s just not my thing. But let me tell you that the three way between Xcor, Throe and the prostitute was sizzling hot. Um, wow! Let’s keep that between us, okay. I don’t want to ruin my pristine reputation here. (very big grin)<br /><br /><b>Final Thoughts</b>:<br />I always worry before I start the newest book by one of my favorite authors. What if my high expectations for their writing are let down? What if the story and I don’t get along? I shouldn’t have worried here. I didn’t feel let down at all. In fact, If I had one complaint, it’s not even a fair one. If only these books could be longer. Even though I’m happy with what I get, I just want more. More romance, more magic, more everything, because she does it so well. I felt as though I only got teasing glimpses of the rest of the gang. It’s not enough. I just want more! That’s how she keeps us hooked, with the teases and the shots of her awesomeness. But that’s okay with me. I’m a loyal customer, and I can’t wait for the next book!<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="18439715760867393231" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText18405133372672455413" style="display:none"> ^^WHAT AN UNLEASHING IT WAS!^^<br /><br /> <b>*Hardly any spoilers, but damn most of you read it anyways*</b><br /><br />Another BDB book has come and gone, and what a book it was. I will say honestly, I was not in love with this book. Totally boning for the characters, but not all weak in the knees for the story. I always love to be reacquainted with the men of the brotherhood, but it seems there is an added brother I did not know about (will discuss later). I will have to break this one down cus there is just so much to freaking write, so freaking much.<br /><br />So we met good old Payne in the last book Lover Mine, she is the sister of my main man Vishous, the daughter of the Bloodletter and the mother of the vampire race, The Scribe Virgin aka *Bitch Face*. So she injured her back and she needs surgery fast, here comes the one and only Manny the human doctor (and I say human lightly).<br /><br /><b>Payne and Manny-</b> From the get go, sparks are flying and feelings are coming out strong. I am talking territorial Manny, all she’s “mine”, and the dark spices scenting the air and shit. Payne is captivated by her healer and it’s apparent to all that feelings are running deep. Only one problem Manny is human, and that my friend is a no, no. So they pull the mind erase trick, but eventually they will need him again and feelings between the two will become deeper.<br /><br />I really loved Manny; he’s like my Butch. I love the attitude and I like how he handles Vishous. He’s so down True. Payne is alright as a character. I feel like I don’t really know her, and it seems all that remains is that she is just Vishous’s twin. I wish there was more time spent on both Manny and Payne. Since it was their freaking book! In the end, I am kinda disappointed in both.<br /><br /><b>Vishous and Butch-</b> Vishous was really pissing me off in the beginning of the book. I just can’t deal with a whiny Vishous, it’s just not him. It seemed forced and fake to me. He was just too much too soon, but in the end, I wanted him naked like I always do. I did love the breakthrough between him and Butch. Those two should have ditched their respected mates a long time ago. Once again, this brought to light, that puff the magic Jane and ocean breeze Marissa is suited elsewhere. I just never understood why those two are not together, and I am happy cus I read the Fanfiction True, cus in my head Butch and Vishous bend each other over.<br /><br /><b>Black Wax-</b> Black Wax, where have you been? You don't call, u don't write, and no appearances on V's chest in like forever. The you show up making an explosion on his c*ck. I applaud you Black Wax.<br /><br /><b>Saxton (the added brother)-</b> What the flying Feck, this guy I tell ya. He irked me so I wrote him a letter.<br /><i></i><p>To Saxton (The Classy Slut),<br />Do you remember that time when you got beat up and brought to the brotherhood mansion? If no? I sure freaking do, I also remember that vampires heal quickly, and so my question is. Why the hell are you still there? I remember a time when you were lusting after Vishous, and being a big shot lawyer to the glymera. So what the hell happened to your house? I know it’s a scary time with the lessers and all that, but Lash is gone and if the aristocrats of the vampire world are reappearing, my guess is that you could head on home. I am really sick and tired of your Tresseme hair and loafers at first meal. We get it, you and Blay are lovers and all that but man you took it too far and can't he dematerialize to your home. Go home Saxton. In no way do I hate you but you kinda pissing me off with your sexiest man alive routine. You know the Sitch with Blay,let him go.<br /><br />Thanks <br />Darien of Team QUAY! (And if you don’t understand team Blay +Quinn)</p><br /><b>Letter discretely placed on his side of the bed.</b><br /><br /><b>Wrath-</b> I was surprised by you for a second there, when you uttered this phrase “I’m also your cocksucking king” to Vishous. If there was cocksucking going on why wasn’t I invited. Did I miss something because I remember clearly it was only you and Beth? Next, my blind king don’t be such a tease. I hear cocksucking and my mind gets away from me.<br /><br /><b>Blay-</b> Tell Saxton to go home. You guys getting it on does not appeal to me. <br /><br /><b>Quinn-</b> My poor baby, he freaking broke my heart. Also, tell Saxton to go home. I just can’t believe the growth he had, I am proud of him and I am looking forward to him getting his shit together and backing Blay up in a corner and bending him over. Had a moment when his story line became a little <b>EFFED UP</b>, and if that is gonna be some complications in the future. Then me and the Warden are gonna have to have a serious talk.<br /><br /><b>To the Prostitute-</b> You very lucky woman. Throe and Xcor at the same time. I hate you, yet I am bowing down to your super awesomeness. Plus, they did deserve that freaking tip, and you should have asked them to kiss. Just throwing it out there. I also wanted a Throe-down, and it Xcor.<br /><br /><b>Veck-</b> I love you, and I want you, and you intrigue me. I like your bad boy styles and I think you could handle the vampire world. I was kinda hoping you would be in it, but I guess the Warden has other plans for you.<br /><br /><b>Feelings-</b> Not my fave book in the series, but it was entertaining. I loved how there is now a story of intrigue. The brotherhood and Xcor and his band of bastards. Its gonna get spicy and not dark spices spicy, unless Layla lands her eyes on Xcor. I wish Manny and Payne got more page time, I don’t feel like I know them too well. The serial spin was alright, took up too much time, but I understand why it was needed, and it worked out well. Even though this book was lacking in awesomeness, it creates a setting for some serious epicness ahead. I am hoping the Warden can deliver, and please stick to maybe two story, three the most and not the twenty-five going on in this book.<br /><br /><b>SideNote-</b> If Manny had orgasm just one more time, I was gonna put his penis to rest. Seriously, you really had all that in you. Needing or not Payne probably got pregnant from default alone.<br /></span>

<div id="review_101483974" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/101483974" />
    <a title="Auntee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/886675-auntee"><img alt="Auntee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1281897695p2/886675.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/101483974?book_show_action=true">May 05, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Auntee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Auntee" href="/user/show/886675-auntee">Auntee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of the series</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=2011_reads">2011_reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer101483974" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4427296631478125079">Loved it. <i>Luuvvvved it.</i> Not a whole heck of a lot going on in this one (in terms of action/fighting the Lessers), but I loved it anyway. I just loved the romance in this one... <br/><br/><i>Lover Unleashed</i> is mainly the vampire Payne (twin sister of Vishous) and (the human) Dr. Manuel Manello's story, and their relationship is <i>hot</i> with a capital <b>H</b>! Oh my, the 45-year-old Manny is in a constant state of arousal in this one whenever he's <i>near</i> Payne.:) He meets her when he's brought in by Doc Jane to operate on</span>
  <span id="freeText4427296631478125079" style="display:none">Loved it. <i>Luuvvvved it.</i> Not a whole heck of a lot going on in this one (in terms of action/fighting the Lessers), but I loved it anyway. I just loved the romance in this one... <br><br><i>Lover Unleashed</i> is mainly the vampire Payne (twin sister of Vishous) and (the human) Dr. Manuel Manello's story, and their relationship is <i>hot</i> with a capital <b>H</b>! Oh my, the 45-year-old Manny is in a constant state of arousal in this one whenever he's <i>near</i> Payne.:) He meets her when he's brought in by Doc Jane to operate on Payne, after <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ she's paralyzed in an accident while sparring with Wrath. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> It's lust at first sight between Payne and her 'healer', and the lust grows and multiplies and turns into need and want and <i>love</i> the more time they spend together. (And Manny has an interesting way of <i>healing</i> Payne...and Payne has an interesting 'effect' on Manny). Even though Manny's head tells him that a relationship between a human and a vampire has nowhere to go, he finds it hard to tear himself away from Payne. Before Payne, Manny didn't have much in his life besides work, and his racehorse Glory. But after meeting Payne, Manny realizes what he's been missing. There's plenty of heat in this relationship, and more than a few problems. But god how I loved the way they worked them out! Lots of surprises in this relationship...and I don't want to give anything else away. Just read it. Once again JR Ward amazes me with her ability to write one <i>erotic</i> romance!<br><br><i>Manny...</i><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/albums/ac3/aunteecr/?action=view&amp;current=l_c8522671e7e64699a28be3ff5f04d343.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380334637i/693938.jpg" alt="Manny Manello,BDB" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This story wasn't all Manny and Payne--there are a few subplots:<br><br> * Vishous and Jane's relationship is in trouble--these two just aren't communicating like they should. Vishous is really messed up, still craving pain, and still dealing with his past and upbringing by the Bloodletter. Jane asks Butch to step in and give Vishous what he needs (no, it's not what you think). Although it nearly breaks his heart, Butch steps up to the plate to help out the friend he loves like a brother.<br><br><i>Vishous...</i><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/albums/ac3/aunteecr/?action=view&amp;current=vishous-2.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380334637i/693939.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br> * Qhuinn. Ah, what can I say? Qhuinn is still kicking himself for not being honest with Blay (and himself). He realizes he may have blown it with Blay, since Blay and Saxton seem to be happy together--or are they? And then there's Layla. How does she figure into the Qhuinn/Blay equation?<br><br><i>Qhuinn...</i><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/albums/ac3/aunteecr/?action=view&amp;current=pic09.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380334637i/693940.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br> * There's a serial killer on the loose in Caldwell, and Detective Jose de la Cruz and his interesting new partner (Thomas DelVecchio--is he a good guy or a bad guy?) are hot on his trail...<br><br> * Annnnnd...there's a new band of vampire soldier 'brothers' in town (or should I say 'band of bastards') led by their disfigured leader (Xcor)-- who had a relationship with V and Payne's twisted father (the Bloodletter)-- and it looks like they'll be trying to challenge the authority of Wrath in future books. But first Xcor has a score to settle with Payne...<br><br> * Annnnd...the relationship between Manny and one of the Brothers is explored. Could Manny and this brother be related? (I'm sure you can guess who this is...)<br><br>Oh yeah, lots of good stuff in this one, written in a style that's unique to JR Ward. This was a very easy read, with no slow parts (lessers, Omega, Scribe Virgin, etc.), plenty of building and building <i>heat</i>, some familiar faces (all the brothers and their shellans were at least mentioned, and a few--Rhage, Wrath, and of course Butch, have speaking parts), some humor, and a hero and heroine that I just <i>adored</i>. Payne was tough yet vulnerable, and very, very likable. Manny was just...hot. I can't put it much plainer than that. I loved every moment of reading about him and Payne.<br><br>Now, while 99% of the book was great, there were a few things that disappointed me a bit. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The book ended a bit abruptly. There was no mating ceremony between Vishous and Jane, which I expected, or between Manny and Payne.:( Should've been an epilogue there. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> A few things were left hanging, which was okay with me (the relationship between Qhuinn and Blay, the serial killer plot, the new vampires in town and what that will mean to the BDB). I'm sure all that will be resolved in future books.<br><br>Whose story is next? It's hard to tell. Will it be Qhuinn and Blay, or will Ward torture them a bit longer? Will it be Tohr, or does he need to grieve for Wellsie a bit more? Will it be someone new? Or maybe a story about Xcor of one of his soldiers (perhaps Throe)? I don't care who it's about--whatever Ward writes, I will read it with absolute relish. The only thing I dislike about Ward's<br>books...is finishing them. What a letdown when you turn the last page and realize that...there's no more. 5 stars</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="4427296631478125079" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_646522094" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/646522094" />
    <a title="• Lisa •" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa"><img alt="• Lisa •" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576172089p2/11963959.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/646522094?book_show_action=true">Jun 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="• Lisa •" class="user" itemprop="url" name="• Lisa •" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa">• Lisa •</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11963959-lisa?shelf=favourite-series">favourite-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer646522094" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15157282558680256007">FIVE UNLEASHED STARS.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426124i/851124._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426124i/851125._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='500' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>What a opening even the prologue sets the scene for an intriguing and exciting story. The series has been gold standard, every story, every character, every piece and part of the journey is astounding. Another five star instalment to add to the growing pile. I'm not sure how she does it but this talented author has delivered once again and now I'm at book nine of the series, I'm flabbergasted that I'm still entertained at five star standard.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426124i/851126._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='500' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>So, what's it all about?<br/>'Lover Unl</span>
  <span id="freeText15157282558680256007" style="display:none">FIVE UNLEASHED STARS.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426124i/851124._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426124i/851125._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What a opening even the prologue sets the scene for an intriguing and exciting story. The series has been gold standard, every story, every character, every piece and part of the journey is astounding. Another five star instalment to add to the growing pile. I'm not sure how she does it but this talented author has delivered once again and now I'm at book nine of the series, I'm flabbergasted that I'm still entertained at five star standard.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426124i/851126._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, what's it all about?<br>'Lover Unleashed' delivers what the title suggests, a female vampire, the twin of Vishous, has been kept lock and key for centuries under the prison of the scribe virgin, in this book we see her being released into the world as we know it, but not without trial, Payne sustains an injury and her life is in grave danger. We are then re introduced to Doctor Manny Manello an experienced human doctor who's skills are required to complete surgery. Once these characters meet we are taken on their journey of finding love and all the obstacles that they face as a vampire falling in love with a human.The story also follows the rest of the brotherhood, we get more insight into the relationship of Vishous and Doctor Jane, the dark side of making a relationship work under the strain of an abused past and we are also updated on the other brothers, So all in all a jam packed, incredible book number nine. <br><br>❤❤<b>“You are perfect for a female." "Not where I come from." "Then they're using the wrong standard.”</b><br><br>❤❤<b>“Sometimes the only way to know how far you'd come was to return to where you once had been.”</b><br><br>What I loved ...<br>Well it just about goes without saying that I completely HEART this authors style of writing and putting a story together, but this story specifically delivered something special, so we have a human male falling for our kick ass female vampire and I loved the connection between the two, this author seriously knows how to create scenes of romance and forever loving. I get so wrapped up in the stories that I'm always desperate to read the next book in the series. 'Lover Unleashed' wraps up perfectly and it delivers the usual heart stopping romance and love and if you like your PNR sizzling hot then this definitely will hit your reading spot.<br><br>Final thoughts ...<br>The brotherhood is a serious addiction, like I have said in previous reviews I never thought I would love a PNR series with a slice of suspense and drama so much. It is not surprising that this author is so popular, the brotherhood and surrounding characters are incredible. So next up book number ten, the bestie buddy read continues, I'm already lining up my five gold stars.<br><br>❤❤<b>“Love can conquer everything but reality.” </b><br><br>❤❤<b>“Why ever are you here?“ she whispered, putting her hands to his face.<br>“Because I love you.” In so many ways, that explained nothing … and told her everything she needed to know.” </b></span>
  <a data-text-id="15157282558680256007" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1370072494" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1370072494" />
    <a title="Sophia Triad" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad"><img alt="Sophia Triad" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591419108p2/44642860.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1370072494?book_show_action=true">Aug 21, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sophia Triad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sophia Triad" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad">Sophia Triad</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=fangywarriorteams">fangywarriorteams</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=1paranormal-lovestories">1paranormal-lovestories</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1370072494" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6634619640138224869"><b>Payne and Dr. Manuel Manello</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>It finally happened, he thought as he burrowed under his shirt and took hold of his heavy cross. All his life he’d wondered why he’d never fallen in love, and now he knew: He’d been waiting for this moment, this woman, this time.<br/>The female is mine, he thought.<br/>And even though that made no sense at all, the conviction was so strong, he couldn’t question it.<br/>“Are you the healer?” she said in a low voice that stopped his heart. “Are you . . . here for me?”<br/>Her words</blockquote></i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText6634619640138224869" style="display:none"><b>Payne and Dr. Manuel Manello</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>It finally happened, he thought as he burrowed under his shirt and took hold of his heavy cross. All his life he’d wondered why he’d never fallen in love, and now he knew: He’d been waiting for this moment, this woman, this time.<br />The female is mine, he thought.<br />And even though that made no sense at all, the conviction was so strong, he couldn’t question it.<br />“Are you the healer?” she said in a low voice that stopped his heart. “Are you . . . here for me?”<br />Her words were heavily accented, gorgeously so, and also a little surprised.<br />“Yeah. I am.” He wrenched off his suit’s coat and threw it into a corner, not giving a shit where the thing landed. <br />“I’m here for you.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br />Manny has never been in love. Or maybe he has never loved anyone at all in his life. He loves his horse of course. And he cared for Jane. But he wasn’t really in love with her. She was mostly his best friend until she died. And then Jane is alive again somehow and she asks him to help with an injured female who cannot feel her legs.<br /><br />Payne used to love being the sparring partner of Wrath, until the king caused a severe injury and now Payne is paralyzed from the waist down. Payne is transported in BDB mansion where she will soon meet a human healer who can fix her. It is a good thing that Manny is a good surgeon (with a god complex someone may add). <br /><br />When Manny and Payne meet, there are sparks everywhere and this is something that Vishous (Payne’s twin brother who didn’t know that he had a twin sister until then) does not like it. Let’s not forget that Manny used to want Jane and this is something that V cannot forget and forgive.<br /><br />I loved Vishous acting as the big, protective brother:<br /><b>
  <blockquote>Jane tightened her arm around his waist. “Are you all right?”<br />He glanced down at his shellan. “I don’t think my sister is old enough to have sex.”<br />“V, she’s the same age you are.”<br />He frowned for a moment. Was she? Or had he been born first?</blockquote>
</b><br />The situation will be resolved when both Payne and Manny declare their love for each other to Vishous.<br /><br />V and Payne:<br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Answer me one thing,” her twin said. <br />“What.” <br />“Do you love the bas—him. Do you love him?” <br />Payne looked back through the glass at the human on the bed. “Yes. I am in love with him. And if you try to dissuade me by the fact that I have not lived yet enough to judge, I say unto you . . . fuck off. I need not know the world to realize my heart’s desire.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br />V and Manny:<br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I love her so damned much,” Manny heard himself say. “That’s my heart right there. That’s my woman.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br />Payne and Manny have the sweetest love story. There is hardly any tension between them. It is just a matter of others to accept it.<br /><br />Welcome Manny in the BDB mansion!<br /><br />Last but not least, welcome Xcor and Band of bastards in the BDB world!</span>
  <a data-text-id="6634619640138224869" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2561643227" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1873086885158133510"><strong>So good and surprising reveals!</strong><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1576904743ra/28644965.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>So much happens in these books it is like a few books in one. The story of Payne and Manny was much better than the than I expected it to be. He was brought in to operate on her after she broke her back and had to be brought to the Mansion from the Sanctuary.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1576904743ra/28644966.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1552367757ra/27191729.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>They feel a connection right away, but she is struggling with being paralyzed since it is like being imprisoned in your body, when she is a warrior and needs to be active. Plus she is finally free of her mother</span>
  <span id="freeText1873086885158133510" style="display:none"><strong>So good and surprising reveals!</strong><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1576904743ra/28644965.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So much happens in these books it is like a few books in one. The story of Payne and Manny was much better than the than I expected it to be. He was brought in to operate on her after she broke her back and had to be brought to the Mansion from the Sanctuary.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1576904743ra/28644966.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1552367757ra/27191729.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They feel a connection right away, but she is struggling with being paralyzed since it is like being imprisoned in your body, when she is a warrior and needs to be active. Plus she is finally free of her mother and Sanctuary, yet stuck in a hospital bed. Prior to the surgery she made V promise to kill her if she ends up stuck that way. Jane knows there is no way Vishous can handle that.<br><br>As it is, Vishous is spiraling. He is crazy angry at the Scribe Virgin (his Mom) already for keeping the fact that she was his Mom from him and giving him to the Bloodletter for all those years growing up, but now finding out that she kept a twin sister from him puts him in a rage. He just wants pain and doesn’t know how to deal.<br><br>Bloodletters other son, Xcor and his group of Vampires, after ridding Europe of Lessers, have come across the Pond to destroy the King. They are setting up a meeting with the Glymera to try to win favor over the Brotherhood. They have also hit the streets slaughtering lessers. Xcor has been searching for Payne ever since she assassinated the Bloodletter to pay her back for killing his father in cold blood.<br><br>Quinn is still pining for Blaylock and Blay is still with Quinn’s cousin, but Loves Quinn. Quinn thinks it is wrong for some reason. Stupid, really, since it seems to be fine to have sex with Men or Women, just not be in a relationship with a man. Crazy. But poor Quinn is so messed up from the fact that his family didn’t love him because he was not perfect and had different colored eyes. I fear it will be a vey long road for him.<br><br><a href="https://www.ilikebooksbest.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a>|<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/wennel" rel="nofollow noopener">Goodreads</a>|<a href="https://www.facebook.com/ilikebooksbest" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a>|<a href="https://smile.amazon.com/gp/profile/amzn1.account.AFFE5A2BGXJQTQMCYHFC4YHV6KFQ?preview=true" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon</a>|<a href="https://www.twitter.com/wendysu020202" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a>|<a href="https://www.bookbub.com/profile/1895823057" rel="nofollow noopener">BookBub</a></span>

<div id="review_108865902" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/108865902" />
    <a title="Tutti Dolci" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2950662-tutti-dolci"><img alt="Tutti Dolci" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1484804213p2/2950662.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/108865902?book_show_action=true">Jun 26, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tutti Dolci" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tutti Dolci" href="/user/show/2950662-tutti-dolci">Tutti Dolci</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2950662-tutti-dolci?shelf=hardcover">hardcover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2950662-tutti-dolci?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2950662-tutti-dolci?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2950662-tutti-dolci?shelf=paranormal-fantasy">paranormal-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer108865902" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5125677316276994537">Oh, my.<br/><br/>What to say?<br/><br/>Ummm...in all honesty? It tanked for me. <br/><br/>I found the storyline weak and Payne, who should've been a kick-ass heroine (ala Xhex, perhaps, but sexier?) was everything BUT. I also found Manny's and (LORD-PLEASE-FORGIVE-ME-FOR-TYPING-THIS) Vishous' story lines to be too neatly wrapped up and tied off with a pretty bow. Furthermore, Qhuinn's premonition? Uh, perhaps I don't recall, but I thought that the only one who could see into the future was V. That felt kind of like it came o</span>
  <span id="freeText5125677316276994537" style="display:none">Oh, my.<br /><br />What to say?<br /><br />Ummm...in all honesty? It tanked for me. <br /><br />I found the storyline weak and Payne, who should've been a kick-ass heroine (ala Xhex, perhaps, but sexier?) was everything BUT. I also found Manny's and (LORD-PLEASE-FORGIVE-ME-FOR-TYPING-THIS) Vishous' story lines to be too neatly wrapped up and tied off with a pretty bow. Furthermore, Qhuinn's premonition? Uh, perhaps I don't recall, but I thought that the only one who could see into the future was V. That felt kind of like it came out of left field. Let's see...what else? I had several issues with this book but mostly it's that it was nowhere near as strong as many of the other books. Hell, I was really disappointed with Phury's book and this one is just a notch BELOW it for me. <br /><br />Yeah, I wasn't fond of it.<br /><br />It didn't even move us along in the BDB world! I don't really care a whole lot about the whole Lesser thing, but I didn't really get too much out of the epic battle that's to come, other than Xcor's potential involvement. Is it that the antagonist in this series will now be a new batch of non-Brotherhood warriors and not so much the Omega's lessers? I am Le Confuzzled. <br /><br />And wait...shouldn't we have gotten a little more insight on Mhurder? For some reason, I thought we'd know more about him in this book. <br /><br />*sigh*<br /><br />Lover Unleashed gets a C- from me (also known as a "Meh") and that's really disappointing because I adore this series as a whole and expected so much more.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5125677316276994537" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_745004533" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/745004533" />
    <a title="Shurrn" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22115857-shurrn"><img alt="Shurrn" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1410564134p2/22115857.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/745004533?book_show_action=true">Oct 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shurrn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shurrn" href="/user/show/22115857-shurrn">Shurrn</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=romance-paranormal">romance-paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=i-lol-moments">i-lol-moments</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=genre-scifi-and-fantasy">genre-scifi-and-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=series-unfinished">series-unfinished</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=z-own-paperback">z-own-paperback</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=i-spells-magic-curses">i-spells-magic-curses</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=favorite-romantic-series">favorite-romantic-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=s-vampires">s-vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=c-bad-ass-bitches">c-bad-ass-bitches</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer745004533" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18178475913311864557"><b>Always a pleasure to see strong females in the BDB series...</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388605519ra/7884340.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Love can conquer everything but reality. Which will win every stinking time."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> Let me start with the following warning: It is impossible to review any book in the Black Dagger Brotherhood Series without mentioning spoilers for all the books which came before it. With that in mind, you might not want to read this review if you haven't read the first eight books in the series...<br/><br/>The BDB Series focuses on a new couple with each</span>
  <span id="freeText18178475913311864557" style="display:none"><b>Always a pleasure to see strong females in the BDB series...</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388605519ra/7884340.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Love can conquer everything but reality. Which will win every stinking time."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> Let me start with the following warning: It is impossible to review any book in the Black Dagger Brotherhood Series without mentioning spoilers for all the books which came before it. With that in mind, you might not want to read this review if you haven't read the first eight books in the series...<br><br>The BDB Series focuses on a new couple with each book, yet keeps the reader updated with all of the other brothers. The plethora of POVs can be a bit daunting at times, but you get used to it once you get this far in the series.<br><br><b>The unofficial breakdown of plot:</b><br>40% Payne &amp; Manny <br>40% Vishous &amp; Jane (who had their own spotlight 4 books ago)<br>8% Lead up of Blay and Qhuinn (Who get their own story in book 11)<br>8% The band of Bastards (Who are a brand new addition to the series)<br>4% Caldwell Cops Jose de la Cruz and his new partner Thomas DelVecchio<br><br><b>Payne</b><br><i>Blooded sister of the Brother Vishous, son of The Bloodletter</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412705319i/11410686._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Payne looked back through the glass at the human on the bed. "Yes. I am in love with him. And if you try to dissuade me by the fact that I have not lived yet enough to judge, I say unto you...fuck off."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> Payne is the twin sister of Vishous. She was kept in forced hibernation by the Scribe Virgin for centuries, and only let out of her cage at the end of Phury's book. She's every bit the warrior that her brother is, and simply does not fit the mold created for Vampire Females.<br><br>At the end of the last book, she was sparring with Wrath on the Other Side when she cracked her head. Payne was paralyzed by the hit, and Wrath managed to bring her back to the mansion in the hopes that she could be healed.<br><br>Unfortunately, Doc Jane is ill-equipped to handle the devastating injury to her spinal cord. Her only choice is to reach out to one of her old contacts in the human world... <br><br><b>Dr. Manuel Manello</b><br><i>Chief of Surgery, Caldwell Medical Center</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412705319i/11410687._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>It finally happened, he thought as he burrowed under his shirt and took hold of his heavy cross. All his life he’d wondered why he’d never fallen in love, and now he knew: He’d been waiting for this moment, this woman, this time. The female is mine, he thought.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> We first met Dr. Manello in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/304027.Lover_Unbound__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___5_" title="Lover Unbound (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #5) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Unbound</a>. He was the Chief of Surgery who had the hots for Jane. The poor guy is brought to the mansion by the ghost of the woman he once cared for. He's asked to operate on a gorgeous woman who isn't real enthusiastic about the idea. If he fails, he's pretty sure that he'll be murdered, and even if she <i>does</i> walk again, her brother might kill Manny just for being around his sister...<br><br>Manny manages to get through the surgery, but his memories are wiped clean by his vampire abductors before he ever has a chance to learn if it was a success. The memory wipe really does a number on the good doctor - he's losing his mind with the vague memories, vivid dreams, headaches, and lost time...<br><br><b>Vishous &amp; Jane</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412709231i/11411457._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I wish I were whole. I wish I could have given you young if you'd wanted them and could conceive them. I wish I could have told you that it killed me when you thought I had been with anyone else. I wish I had spent the last year waking up every night and telling you that I loved you. I wish I had mated you properly the evening you came back to me from dead. I wish. . ." <br>"I wish I were half as strong as you are and I wish I deserved you. And. . . that's about it."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> Vishous was stunned to discover that he had a twin sister and heartbroken to realize that she might die before he had the opportunity to know her.<br><br>In the wake of these revelations, V's psyche is taking a tumble. His relationship with Jane is deteriorating rapidly, and his self destructive tendencies have shifted into high gear.<br><br>Apparently the solution to V's internal suffering is to let go with a good dose of physical pain. Enter Butch and the infamous black candled condo filled with all the trappings of V's former BDSM lifestyle. I think many readers have been fantasizing about that particular scene for a while now...<br><br><b>Blay &amp; Qhuinn</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412712081i/11411789._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>But by God, he was going to stop running from his cowardice. He had to own his shit - even if it made him hate himself to the core. Because maybe if he did, he'd stop trying to distract himself with sex and drinking, and figure out what he <u>did</u> want.<br>Apart from Blay, that was.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> We pop into Qhuinn's life several times throughout this story. He's still convinced that he'll never be with Blay even though he knows he will never love anyone as much as him... He's been whoring and brooding and running himself ragged to the point that John Matthew finally has to set him straight... <br><br>Qhuinn vows to turn over a new leaf, stop whoring around and get his shit together. His growing friendship with the Chosen Layla is obviously leading to something bigger. I suppose we'll just have to wait and see what happens to the poor naive girl when Blay &amp; Qhuinn stop denying what's between them...<br><br>For the love of The Scribe Virgin - I can't wait for their fucking book!<br><br><b>Xcor</b><br>&amp; his merry Band of Bastards<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412709231i/11411458._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Wrath and the Brotherhood had too long ruled this continent, and to what end? The Lessening Society persisted. The Vampire population had scattered. And those arrogant, flabby, feckless humans where everywhere.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> Where previous books in the series might have provided a POV to see what was happening in the <i>Lessening</i> Society, this book introduced us to a brand new enemy in the Vampire War. The Band of Bastards - chiefly comprised of warrior males who trained with The Bloodletter but didn't make the cut to become members of the Black Dagger Brotherhood. They have a serious chip on their collective shoulders from being rejected by the BDB, and their leader, Xcor, has a few issues of his own...<br><br>Turns out, Payne escaped from the other side to commit patricide a few hundred years ago. Her completely justifiable, kinda badass, right in front of the Band of Bastards murder of The Bloodleter left them hungry for revenge.<br><br>Xcor arrives in Caldwell looking for a way to dethrone the Blind King. I guess we'll just have to read on if we're going to find out how that goes ;)<br><br><b>Complete honesty:</b><br>I've been steadily chipping away at this series for one reason - I'm dying to see Blay and Qhuinn get their HEA. It kills me to know that Ward is going to drag these two through some awful shit before we get there. She systematically strips her characters of all dignity before granting them their own book.<br><br>I've been a bit underwhelmed with the series for several books. I haven't felt satisfied after finishing a BDB book since Z's story... and that was book <i>four</i>!<br><br>I hate how angsty and pansy-assed some of these warrior vampires can be...<br>I hate that we keep replaying the "I love you but I push you away" theme over and over...<br>I'm getting aggravated by the constant deluge of brands...<br>I'll never believe that an 800 year old vampire texts like a 14 year old girl...<br><br>*sigh*<br><br>But so help me, I'm oddly in love with this damn series. I seem to grant JR Ward a lot of slack that I might not give to other authors. Mostly, I'm just determined to get to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13570854.Lover_at_Last__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___11_" title="Lover at Last (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #11) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover At Last</a> - Blay &amp; Qhuinn's book... We'll see if I continue after that...<br><br><b>
  <u>My Other Reviews in the Black Dagger Brotherhood Series:</u>
</b><br>1. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/42899.Dark_Lover__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___1_" title="Dark Lover (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #1) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Dark Lover</a> - <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/728410865" rel="nofollow noopener">My Review</a><br>2. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/35729.Lover_Eternal__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___2_" title="Lover Eternal (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #2) by J.R.   <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1389986026s/42899.jpg" alt="Dark Lover (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #1) by J.R. Ward" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/35729.Lover_Eternal__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___2_" title="Lover Eternal (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #2) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_2011455634" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2011455634" />
    <a title="warhawke" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25494927-warhawke"><img alt="warhawke" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1431835527p2/25494927.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2011455634?book_show_action=true">May 26, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="warhawke" class="user" itemprop="url" name="warhawke" href="/user/show/25494927-warhawke">warhawke</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Vamps lovers</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=paranormal-sci-fi-fantasy">paranormal-sci-fi-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=romance-love">romance-love</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2011455634" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1131769975344439589"><b>Genre: </b> Paranormal Romance/Urban Fantasy<br/><b>Type: </b>Book 9 of Black Dagger Brotherhood series<br/><b>POV: </b>Third Person<br/><b>Rating: </b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454075031i/17913446.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1496093547i/22881349._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>For hundreds of years Payne was confined to the Other Side. Desperate to be free, she took an extreme measure that landed her in human world but in critical condition.<br/><br/>Dr. Manny Manello was a successful and established surgeon. He had everything he could possibly wanted, but still reeling from his loss of the woman who captured his heart. When an unexpected encounter thrown him into th</span>
  <span id="freeText1131769975344439589" style="display:none"><b>Genre: </b> Paranormal Romance/Urban Fantasy<br><b>Type: </b>Book 9 of Black Dagger Brotherhood series<br><b>POV: </b>Third Person<br><b>Rating: </b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454075031i/17913446.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1496093547i/22881349._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For hundreds of years Payne was confined to the Other Side. Desperate to be free, she took an extreme measure that landed her in human world but in critical condition.<br><br>Dr. Manny Manello was a successful and established surgeon. He had everything he could possibly wanted, but still reeling from his loss of the woman who captured his heart. When an unexpected encounter thrown him into the unknown, he must decide what's best for his life.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453882133i/17883711.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I rarely do back to back series reading. But what happened in last book got me intrigued, I just had to continue.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>The truth was, he loved her. Completely and forever. But that was the curse of all this for them both, he suspected.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>While I felt sorry for Manny in past books, I never really cared about him. I'm glad I actually ended up liking him in this book. I like seeing through his eyes the confusion and the wonder of vampires and the Brotherhood life.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>She was a female who didn’t fit in anywhere, a warrior stuck within the tepid skin of a Chosen’s body</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>I've always like Payne since she was first introduced in the series. Even on the Other Side, she was such a badass character. And here we get to see her vulnerability. However as much as I like seeing her flip side, I also wanted more of her badassery (which only appeared at the very end).<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1496093547i/22881350.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I like Manny and Payne together and their storyline was engaging. However, I feel like V and Jane's story overpower the main characters. Also, I don't really see much purpose in the sub story of Butch's former partner and the new guy.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>If Xcor needed some blood to tide him over, he would get it from this woman, or another.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>Xcor is a new character introduced in this book. I like the potential, but I don't like how he simply accepted the issue at the end considering his mindset throughout the book. I also felt deprived of Murdher which is one of the reasons I wanted to read this book thinking he'd make an appearance.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>She had the Bloodletter’s iron will not just in her face or her eyes or her body. It was in her soul.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>Lover Unleashed is a story of overcoming obstacles and standing proud of who you are. I'm hoping the next book will continue with the potential new direction in the series<br><br><i><b>P.S.:</b> Is it wrong that I still have hope for V and Butch? Haha!</i><br><br><br><b>Standalone Books in the series:</b><br><i>Must be read in order</i><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/42899.Dark_Lover__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___1_" title="Dark Lover (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #1) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1429676285s/42899.jpg" alt="Dark Lover (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #1) by J.R. Ward" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/35729.Lover_Eternal__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___2_" title="Lover Eternal (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #2) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1300845974s/35729.jpg" alt="Lover Eternal (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #2) by J.R. Ward" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/42900.Lover_Awakened__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___3_" title="Lover Awakened (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #3) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">
