        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer607553390" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2153034315701456610"><b>5 Stars!!!!!</b> <i>(Duh! like I could give it any less!)</i><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/d04fda40-9340-4c85-9054-a1c79daec1f4_zps61385c09.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420405i/833951.jpg' alt=' photo d04fda40-9340-4c85-9054-a1c79daec1f4_zps61385c09.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I will join the club and say that I am completely OBSESSED with these books and all things BDB! If you haven’t read this series, <b>seriously</b>, get to it! <br/><br/>On to the review!!!<br/><br/>This is Manny and Payne’s story. We met Manny several books ago. He is the chief of surgery and friends with Jane. Then there is Payne. Payne is Vishous’ long lost twin sister he never knew about. An unlikely pair, but they work nonetheless. <br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/6cba1c1c-68d5-4e2e-8d0e-e2feea23366d_zpse4b93138.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420405i/833952.jpg' alt=' photo 6cba1c1c-68d5-4e2e-8d0e-e2feea23366d_zpse4b93138.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>When we last saw Payne in book</span>
  <span id="freeText2153034315701456610" style="display:none"><b>5 Stars!!!!!</b> <i>(Duh! like I could give it any less!)</i><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/d04fda40-9340-4c85-9054-a1c79daec1f4_zps61385c09.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420405i/833951.jpg" alt=" photo d04fda40-9340-4c85-9054-a1c79daec1f4_zps61385c09.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I will join the club and say that I am completely OBSESSED with these books and all things BDB! If you haven’t read this series, <b>seriously</b>, get to it! <br><br>On to the review!!!<br><br>This is Manny and Payne’s story. We met Manny several books ago. He is the chief of surgery and friends with Jane. Then there is Payne. Payne is Vishous’ long lost twin sister he never knew about. An unlikely pair, but they work nonetheless. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/6cba1c1c-68d5-4e2e-8d0e-e2feea23366d_zpse4b93138.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420405i/833952.jpg" alt=" photo 6cba1c1c-68d5-4e2e-8d0e-e2feea23366d_zpse4b93138.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>When we last saw Payne in book #8, she was brought over from the other side and introduced to her brother Vishous. She has always kept an eye out for him. She has fought for him, killed for him, and he didn’t even know she existed. Payne has a major injury. One that has left her paralyzed. Payne is a true warrior at heart and she doesn’t want to live like that. So Vishous and Jane bring in the only person they know can possibly help her. The brilliant surgeon, Dr. Manuel Manello. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/5ff2c4ee-d00d-4124-910a-f1185ba0e2af_zps49153d28.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420405i/833953.jpg" alt=" photo 5ff2c4ee-d00d-4124-910a-f1185ba0e2af_zps49153d28.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Manny is more than a little shocked to see Jane. She was one of his best friends, and he was still grieving her loss. But he will do anything to help her, so he agrees to operate on Payne. He doesn’t know what Payne is at first, but he knows she is different. They have this straight up insta-love/connection. Payne has lived most of her life like a Chosen, she has never had a man. Manny has had many women, but he has never felt like this. Never felt the urge to settle down and just be with someone. He feels that for Payne. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“You are perfect for a female."<br>"Not where I come from."<br>"Then they're using the wrong standard.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/LoverUnleashed-cresst_zps79055a31.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420405i/833954.jpg" alt=" photo LoverUnleashed-cresst_zps79055a31.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>They don’t care what others think of their unconventional union. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Yes. I am in love with him. And if you try to dissuade me by the fact that I have not lived yet enough to judge, I say unto you...fuck off.” <br><br>‘I love her so damn much, thats my heart right there. My woman.’<br>‘Word.’</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/15351657-cfa2-4ee8-b16f-0ecac8a4f333_zps6cc9b577.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420405i/833955.jpg" alt=" photo 15351657-cfa2-4ee8-b16f-0ecac8a4f333_zps6cc9b577.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I could go on and on about the story line for this book. Theres always SO MUCH going on in these things! Payne and Manny have a unique relationship. Once they figured things out, they were really perfect together. I loved the ending, I thought it made sense <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I liked that they didn’t automatically turn him, like Butch. And speaking of BUTCH- HOLY COW!!! Butch and Manny are half brothers??? Didn’t see that coming, but a cool twist!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> It was great to get a little more Qhuinn, looking forward to his book, a long with seeing some of the other brothers! <br><br><br>Let me just say that I loved Manny and Payne’s story. I really did. It was sweet, romantic and I really enjoyed it. But the <u>VERY BEST</u> part of the book.... (If you know me at all, I’m sure you’ve already guessed it...)<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/ce5a100c-c32e-453c-b752-1fee10e73941_zpse4113a2f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794322i/590534.jpg" alt=" photo ce5a100c-c32e-453c-b752-1fee10e73941_zpse4113a2f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/a2851e72-f708-4078-8cdc-91190515c350_zps45c793c5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420405i/833956.jpg" alt=" photo a2851e72-f708-4078-8cdc-91190515c350_zps45c793c5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>YES! There was so much <b>Vishous</b> (and Jane) in this story! It was almost like getting a second V book and I couldn’t have been happier about that! Vishous goes off the edge a little in this one, but he comes back better then ever! I cried, I laughed, I cried some happy tears, I totally swoooooned- all because of Vishous! Loved getting in to his head- <br><b>For shit’s sake, it wasn’t<br>like there was a twelve-step for being the Scribe Virgin’s<br>kid:<br>Hi, I’m Vishous. I’m her son and I’ve been her son for<br>three hundred years.<br>HI, VISHOUS.<br>She’s done a head job on me again, and I’m trying not<br>to go to the Other Side and scream bloody murder at her.<br>WE UNDERSTAND, VISHOUS.<br>And on the bloody note, I’d like to dig up my father<br>and kill him all over again, but I can’t. So I’m just going to<br>try to keep my sister alive even though she’s paralyzed,<br>and attempt to fight the urge to find some pain so I can<br>deal with this Payne.<br>YOU’RE A STRAIGHT-UP PUSSY, VISHOUS, BUT WE SUPPORT<br>YOUR SORRY ASS.</b><br>Sorry but that quote was just hilarious! <br><br>I could make this review go on forever, but I am going to stop here and just say this: Another AMAZING BDB book! Sorry if this is all over the place, these books are impossible to review, just too much! But I LOVE IT! Can’t wait until next Friday! </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="2153034315701456610" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer300337038" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer71025056298426534"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>This was more than just being alive. This was to live.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>Lover Unleashed is the only book in the series I read only twice. Sadly now, for the second read, I was even more bored than I was for the first time.<br/><br/>Jane and Vishous’s storyline captivated me again: witnessing their struggles after their ‘happily ever after’, and seeing them finally finding some peace by the help and the unfaltering friendship of Butch.<br/><br/>Qhuinn and Blay's story goes on, and it's heartbreaking: the tension between t</span>
  <span id="freeText71025056298426534" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>This was more than just being alive. This was to live.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Lover Unleashed is the only book in the series I read only twice. Sadly now, for the second read, I was even more bored than I was for the first time.<br><br>Jane and Vishous’s storyline captivated me again: witnessing their struggles after their ‘happily ever after’, and seeing them finally finding some peace by the help and the unfaltering friendship of Butch.<br><br>Qhuinn and Blay's story goes on, and it's heartbreaking: the tension between them, their sadness, and their resignation are saddening.<br><br>In Payne and Manny’s story there is not enough potential that would be enough for a 500-page-long book. I was bored by Payne’s colorless personality. As she spent almost her whole life “under her mother’s care”, there is no long backstory for her.<br>Manny is just an average human.  Okay, he is a brilliant surgeon, with the body of John Cena, but still. His continuous headaches and continuous hard-ons are annoying. Constant erection, and “sex as a medicine” don’t equal sizzling chemistry.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1540130217i/26480006._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jose de la Cruz and Veck DelVecchio’s storyline is utterly unnecessary, and it obviously appears just because of the <i>Fallen Angels</i> spin-off.<br><br>Though I was bored by Xcor, his old-fashioned ways, and old-fashioned buddies, his nobleness surprised me.<br><br><b>All in all.</b> The sidelines of Vishous-Butch-Jane, and Qhuinn and Blay are captivating, and essential regarding the series. But the other storylines, including the main one, left me uninterested.<br><br>Vishous-Butch-Jane: 5 stars<br>Qhuinn and Blay: 5 stars<br>Payne and Manny: 1 stars<br>Other secondary storylines: 2 stars<br><br><a href="http://exinasreadings.tumblr.com/tagged/Lover-Unleashed" rel="nofollow noopener">My favorite quotes.</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="71025056298426534" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1011433151?book_show_action=true">Jul 30, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amy | Foxy Blogs" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amy | Foxy Blogs" href="/user/show/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs">Amy | Foxy Blogs</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Amy | Foxy Blogs by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/13095060-beverly">Beverly</a>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=2014-books">2014-books</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1011433151" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16770684543420387654">Ms. Ward sure knows how to write forbidden romance and the proof is in this series. For those who haven't read any books from this series keep in mind these vampires always have <b>insta love</b>. Insta-love is something I hate but for some reason it doesn't bother me in this series.<i> Go figure.</i><br/><br/><b>How do you eat an elephant?</b><i> One bit at a time.</i><b> This series is a beast.</b> I started at the end of April working my way through it. Spending each weekend reading one book from this series with my book twin, Bev. We'v</span>
  <span id="freeText16770684543420387654" style="display:none">Ms. Ward sure knows how to write forbidden romance and the proof is in this series. For those who haven't read any books from this series keep in mind these vampires always have <b>insta love</b>. Insta-love is something I hate but for some reason it doesn't bother me in this series.<i> Go figure.</i><br><br><b>How do you eat an elephant?</b><i> One bit at a time.</i><b> This series is a beast.</b> I started at the end of April working my way through it. Spending each weekend reading one book from this series with my book twin, Bev. We've spent a lot of time bonding over the <b>Triple D threat</b> -&gt; <b>d</b>eliciously <b>d</b>escriptive <b>d</b>ongs. <br><br>I love that we got glimpses of Qhuinn and Blay. When Bev and I started reading these books I informed her that I'm not a m/m reader and I will most likely skip book 11. <b>FORGET THAT</b>...I'm jonesing for their book now. One more book before we FINALLY get their love story.<br><br>I wasn't sure if I'd like <b> Manny and Payne's</b> love story since Manny wasn't one of the brothers but instead a human. I was pleasantly surprised by how much I enjoyed this book. Overall, for the series, I've given all the books at least 4 stars even though some books I really didn't care for (Butch, Phury and Rehv) because there were other stories going on within the book that brought the rating up for me. Had it just been the main story the book would have gotten a lower rating.<br><br><b>FORBIDDEN ROMANCE -&gt; 'After all, you can't help who you fall for.'</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398400054i/9409981._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <u>Cheat sheet for the brotherhood</u>
  </i>
</b>: <br><b>Wrath</b>: last pure-blood vampire in existence. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/42899.Dark_Lover__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___1_" title="Dark Lover (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #1) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Dark Lover</a>(#1) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17703290.The_King__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___12_" title="The King (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #12) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">The King</a> (#12) {Wrath &amp; Beth}<br>♥Beth♥: is <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Darius <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> daughter. She's Wrath's shellan (wife) and is half-breed. She has a pet- kitty named, Boo. <br><br><b>Rhage</b>: is the strongest and most beautiful of the Brothers. Nicknamed "Hollywood." <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/35729.Lover_Eternal__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___2_" title="Lover Eternal (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #2) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Eternal</a> (#2) {Rhage &amp; Mary}<br>♥Mary♥: when she meet Rhage she works at a legal office and volunteers for suicide hotline. She's Rhage's shellan. She has <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[leukemia <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><br><b>Zsadist</b>: has a twin, Phury. Described as "ruined, not broken." <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/42900.Lover_Awakened__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___3_" title="Lover Awakened (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #3) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Awakened</a> (#3) {Zsadist &amp; Bella}<br>♥Bella♥: is Mary's neighbor. She has a friendship with Mary and John. Rehvenge is her older brother. She's Zsadist's shellan. <br><br><b>Butch/Dhestroyer</b>: is the only human male ever to be allowed within the Brotherhood. Nickname "Cop." <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/42898.Lover_Revealed__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___4_" title="Lover Revealed (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #4) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Revealed</a> (#4) {Butch &amp; Marissa}<br>♥Marissa♥: is beautiful and has spent 300 years servicing the king with her blood. Sort of the King's shellan (there was nothing intimate between them). Unwanted. Finally becomes Butch's shellan. <br><br><b>Vishous</b>: is the smartest Brother, and the one who is specially gifted/cursed. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/304027.Lover_Unbound__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___5_" title="Lover Unbound (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #5) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Unbound</a> (#5) {Vishous &amp; Jane}<br>♥Jane♥: human surgeon who becomes the brotherhood's private surgeon.<br><br><b>Phury</b>: Zsadist's twin brother and loyal to his brother. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1240662.Lover_Enshrined__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___6_" title="Lover Enshrined (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #6) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Enshrined</a> (#6) {Phury &amp; Cormia}<br>♥Cormia♥: Chosen.<br><br><b>Rehvenge</b>: brother-in-law to Zsadist. He's half symphath and owner of a night club. Drug lord and pimp. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5098079.Lover_Avenged__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___7_" title="Lover Avenged (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #7) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Avenged</a> (#7) {Rehvenge &amp; Ehlena}<br>♥Ehlena♥: a nurse at Haver's clinic. Later works with Ehlena as a nurse for the brotherhood.<br><br><b>John Matthew/Tehrror</b>: is <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ the reincarnation of Darius. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7046495.Lover_Mine__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___8_" title="Lover Mine (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #8) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Mine</a> (#8){JM &amp; Xhex}<br>♥Xhex♥: a symphath assassin.<br><br><b>Dr. Manuel "Manny" Manello</b>: is Chief of Surgery at St. Francis Hospital. Orthopedic surgeon. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8492319.Lover_Unleashed__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___9_" title="Lover Unleashed (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #9) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Unleashed</a> (#9){Manny &amp; Payne}<br>♥Payne♥: V's twin and daughter of the Scribe Virgin and the Bloodletter. <br><br><b>Tohrment</b>: best friends with Darius and JM's pseudo dad <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10993282.Lover_Reborn__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___10_" title="Lover Reborn (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #10) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Reborn</a> (#10)<br>♥Wellsie♥: is Tohrment's shellan. She has a special place in her heart for John. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[She is killed while pregnant <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><br><b>Qhuinn</b>: has mismatched eyes. Color-blind. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13570854.Lover_at_Last__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___11_" title="Lover at Last (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #11) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover at Last</a> (#11)<br><br><b>Blaylock/"Blay"</b>: gentleman<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13570854.Lover_at_Last__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___11_" title="Lover at Last (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #11) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover at Last</a> (#11)<br><br><b>SERIES:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/42899.Dark_Lover__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___1_" title="Dark Lover (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #1) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1974374386" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3546447664844877896">Completing this book has been a long time coming. I have picked it up and put it down many times. And honestly, I don't really know why. Nothing really spoke to me or captured my attention. It was just okay.<br/><br/>I still have every intention of continuing on with the series. I just hope I do it sooner rather than later.<br/><br/>3 stars!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14941429290019404747"><b>* * * * * 5 <i>Thank Goodness</i> Stars * * * * *</b><br/><br/>I have been struggling through these last few books, but I have been continuing since my <b>Twinie Amy</b> has been dragging me along. I am so thankful she has been, because I absolutely <b>loved</b> this one!<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1406122733ra/10507578.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>All of the BDB books have side stories and this is something that has driven me a little crazy in the past, but I loved the side stories in this one. I felt these side stories were relevant and because they focused on the Brothers I actually cared what was happen</span>
  <span id="freeText14941429290019404747" style="display:none"><b>* * * * * 5 <i>Thank Goodness</i> Stars * * * * *</b><br><br>I have been struggling through these last few books, but I have been continuing since my <b>Twinie Amy</b> has been dragging me along. I am so thankful she has been, because I absolutely <b>loved</b> this one!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1406122733ra/10507578.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>All of the BDB books have side stories and this is something that has driven me a little crazy in the past, but I loved the side stories in this one. I felt these side stories were relevant and because they focused on the Brothers I actually cared what was happening. Even the stories that were not directly related were important. <br><br>Now let’s focus on our main story – Manny and Payne. <br><br>Manny…love, love, love…he was sweet, caring and protective of Payne. Payne, V’s twin sister, was strong, loving, independent and I loved her too! She was selfless with Manny, and was willing to risk everything to keep him safe and happy. <b>One of my favorite BDB couples for sure!</b><br><br>On a side note…only 1 more book until I finally get to the epic story of Qhuinn and Blay!<br></span>

<div id="review_198431178" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/198431178" />
    <a title="Celeste" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6037732-celeste"><img alt="Celeste" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/198431178?book_show_action=true">Aug 14, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Celeste" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Celeste" href="/user/show/6037732-celeste">Celeste</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer198431178" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16379452982986607223">*** Spoilers ***<br/><br/>When I originally heard on JR Ward’s message board and last year’s signing for Crave, that she intended to redeem V and Jane’s relationship through telling Payne and Manny’s story in Lover Unleashed, I became more anxious than typical for its release. If I recall correctly, I understood from comments written and/or stated by JR that she wanted to correct how she left Lover Unbound where V felt more for Butch than Jane, hence why people didn’t have closure on the V/Butch scenario.</span>
  <span id="freeText16379452982986607223" style="display:none">*** Spoilers ***<br /><br />When I originally heard on JR Ward’s message board and last year’s signing for Crave, that she intended to redeem V and Jane’s relationship through telling Payne and Manny’s story in Lover Unleashed, I became more anxious than typical for its release. If I recall correctly, I understood from comments written and/or stated by JR that she wanted to correct how she left Lover Unbound where V felt more for Butch than Jane, hence why people didn’t have closure on the V/Butch scenario.<br /><br />Don’t get me wrong, JR Ward is an amazing writer and has me sucked into her stories it so much that it was torture waiting until the next book was in my hands, devouring every word. I support her adamantly and still I’m a fan as well as place her at the very top of my most loved authors, however, Lover Unleashed just did not deliver what I thought it might and left me feeling empty. <br /><br />In my opinion, the continuity was a big factor in my reaction and at times took me out of the story completely. I’m not usually this technical because for me if the story draws me in, slip ups in continuity, editing, etc. has no bearings on me and therefore are moot to even mention. Yet the V/Jane story felt like sequences were out of order when taking into consideration the scenes from Lover Unbound and ricked havoc with my enjoyment. In many ways, it felt like JR tried to rewrite Vishous and Jane’s story.<br /><br />The first discrepancy that had me scratching my head was on page 67 where she wrote about V’s visions “His visions were exclusively of deaths – those of his brothers and Wrath and their shellans and children. ……. So what he saw now was not the future.” In my opinion, this almost destroyed the world building for me mainly because V’s visions were so impactful from DL and they were not all about deaths and everyone, including himself, had full confidence in them. It’s why Wrath allowed Butch in the brotherhood; V telling Rhage in Lover Eternal about his mate being a virgin and adamantly stating his visions were never wrong; V saved Wrath with the warning of dogs; V saw Butch in the woods which lead him to trick Butch into drinking his blood; etc. There was only one exception – visions pertaining to him. That would easily have explained why he never saw Payne prior to when she crossed over to kill Bloodletter, and being on the other side I’m sure helped blocked those visions too. Get the pic?<br /><br />Pg 109 The suspicion V would/could cheat and Jane thinking V wasn’t happy. In LU, V was all over her in the bedroom after he released her memories and was smiling like the damn Chesire Cat. I can’t even count the number of times JR wrote he smiled compared to his reaction when he wasn’t around Jane – Z talking about it even in Father Mine how happy he was and that was way before the clinic was ever built. Truly, nine books leading up to Lover Unleashed, the founding consistency was that while yes males could and had taken multiple shellans, the warriors bonding came across depicted as being stronger. So much for the bonded male theory and rather cut off their nuts than sleep with another person if you asked me. Not to mention it really minimized all the feelings depicted in Lover Unbound between V and Jane imo. Correct me if I’m wrong, but in LU, V even revealed when he was going to accept the position of Primale, there was a cream that would make him have an erection to service the Chosen therefore eliminating the problem of him only getting an erection for Jane. This doesn’t sound like a bonded male that could cheat. And Butch, who is a bonded male himself, thinking the same about his bestie just felt completely wrong as if Ward had forgotten what her world building was about.<br /><br />Pg 116 Jane says V never talked about his past, only once. And that she felt he favored blooded lovers. Seriously? How many of us remember the “Oatmeal” convo Jane had with V in bed and then V opened up about his castration and tattoo? *bounces in seat with arm flailing over head* Oooo ooo Me Mr. Carter. Mr. Carter!!! And as for favoring blooded lovers, this is another place where the sequences felt out of order. I could see her feeling that right after the penthouse was revealed to her, but not months after being together with him. Not when you look at context of how V was so happy at the end of Lover Unbound after Rhage had walked into a ghostly Jane and then when she left, he was smiling. (almost a mirror image of Butch and Marissa at the morning table earlier in the book that V envied.)<br /><br />Pg 128 V tells Butch he needs a Dom and there was no one he could trust but Butch. Was I the only one that had a double take? That was what made V and Jane’s moment in the penthouse so SPECIAL because that was the only thing he could give her – his submission and trust. For me, JR completely rewrote their story and gave Butch more value than Jane and completely took from what Ward had established in Lover Unbound. Now if it had happened when he was spiraling in LU before Jane, for me then it would have had a different impact. So for me this didn’t fit where it was written in at.<br /><br />Butch being a “midget” in comparison to V that Butch’s clothes didn’t fit V. *Bangs head into keyboard* When Butch transitioned V, Z, and Phury could only comment on how big a motherfucker Butch was. When V meet Marissa in the game room later on when Butch couldn’t, V wanted to dress up to do it and WORE one of Butch’s shirts. Another depiction that seem to be from an earlier book.<br /><br />Pg 153 Jane got the watered down version of him. The only thing Jane did not see (or was written) was V as a Dom other than the bathroom scene. IIRC, I believe V even stated he was more open with Jane than even his brothers and she accepted him. Wasn’t that another key point of their relationship in LU?<br /><br />Pg 216 It’s NOT in Jane to do what V wants. Penthouse…. What did she do? She knew V needed it, wanted to give it to her and she gave it to him. And he came like a geyser more than once. Granted she is a novice Domme and that was her first experience, but it was his first time as a Sub too. V never came across as a masochistic needing pain/endorphins for a high; rather he needed to inflict it. Yes I realize he needed to be broken but why if he always had to be in control, and long for the control did he come to this conclusion and how did he know it would work relying on yet another novice, Butch? Maybe it’s just me not understanding that POV.<br /><br />Pg 242 V asked Butch not to be a hero and let the Brothers handle the fight. What happened when in Lover Eternal, V didn’t stop Butch from entering in a fight with just guns when he was human and later when Butch became the Dhestroyer he was running to the lesser or the Scribe Virgin confirming him into the Brotherhood? That he was on rotation? I’m sorry for me JR tried to rewrite Butch over in my mind too in this book. He was just as big as the brothers and just as fierce. In this book he came out more like he was human. Again this scene actually felt like it belonged in an earlier BDB book.<br /><br />Pg 243 V didn’t want to lose Butch. Wth? It felt like V was emasculated.<br /><br /><br />Ok… from here on out I stopped listing page numbers but I will get to the rest of the points.<br /><br />Enough with the crossover. There was hardly any mention of any other brothers with the exception of cameo appearance of Phury, and mention of them in the ambush, but more than enough mention of Delvecchio, Del a Cruz, and the murderer. It became more a selling pitch for her next book in her fallen angel series, Envy rather than setting up for the next BDB book. I don’t like being manipulated into reading another series in hopes of seeing BDB considering I could leave the fallen angels behind unless she move Lassiter over their world. Nothing will come of Del a Cruz supposedly according to JR comment at a signing – oh well. Hope something comes of the murderer or maybe he will be used like the ghost hunters to bring in Murhder in Lover Mine. Will these three becoming back – Del a Cruz, murderer, and ghost hunters? It used to be that JR never mentioned anything frivolously but, and I could be wrong, it appears she utilized them so much a person was left going “huh?” Each could have been removed and neither would have impacted the story. <br /><br /><br />The band of Bastards - oh damn, I have a new love. It was the only time that I felt that JR even remotely sounded like herself from earlier works with except for writing Qhuinn/Blay.<br /><br /><br />Xcor and his bastards leaving lessers hacked up. Why? Obviously the Brothers recognized his handy work but why wouldn’t the bastards kill as she stated that they had eradicated the lessers from the old country? Did I miss something?<br /><br />The one hot sex scene was the threesome. What happened to all the raw sex that kept the pages burning up? Mostly watered down. Not a page turner.<br /><br />Layla having been trained to be an Eros, to be used for pleasure, and conditioned to serve the Brotherhood (remember Mary’s shock over Layla’s willingness to see herself as an “object to be handled” p319 Lover Eternal) would be so easily to fall for Qhuinn still seemed out of placed. She was so strong and mature with Rhage and Mary and in control of her emotions. <br /><br />On the note of action, this book was severely lacking. One fight? And the brothers got their asses handed to them and no beast out of Rhage? Just didn’t seem to fit. Not that they lost, but how did they lose? The action was glossed over and this had always been one of JR’s strong points in the other books.<br /><br />Jane crying in the clinic. Really? What happened to that bad ass chick in LU who knuckled down like Manny and detached herself to save lives then crumble afterwards? Who didn’t cry at her sister’s funeral?<br /><br />What happened to V’s ability to reading mind’s and needing to have rap music pumping to block out others’ thoughts? He never read anyone’s mind. Another rule broken? Another rewrite?<br /><br />And the paranormal element was nonexistent. To me, these vamps were more human than supernatural. No feeding required after being injured – who did V use? No bursts of cold or heat. No locks being locked, candles being lit? <br /><br />Then there’s the issue of Manny “feeding” Payne. We are left thinking that Manny’s blood satisfied a major world building parameter of the vamps necessity to feed from the opposite sex of their species. Is Manny the exception now? <br /><br />V not caring if his pants was removed in the clinic? He was so obsessed with not being seen even being injured would he really have forgotten this and not panicked? <br /><br /><br />Why did Payne think V had died? Did I miss the explanation? I know on Facebook and on her board, JR posted that No ‘One gave her a seeing bowl and that was how she kept track of V and how she saw the abusiveness of Bloodletter and the scene was deleted for flow, yet there is no explanation as to how she came to believe that.<br /><br />	LOVER MINE, pg. 545-546<br /> <br />	"My twin is long passed unto the Fade." <br /> <br />	(Payne is with No'One and Jane at the Brotherhood's training center.)<br /> <br />	LOVER UNLEASHED, pg. 115<br /> <br />	"The seeing bowls have allowed me to watch him (V) through all the seasons of his life. And I daresay that this time, with you, is by far the best."<br />	<br />Ok, now we get into the V / Butch deal. A person who is a novice or a virgin to BDSM as in the case of Butch would not know how to put V in that rig with the tubing. <br /><br />V feared the mask that did not allow a person to see, really breathe, or hear. IIRC, did V not offer Jane a mask and she said no because she had to be able to see his eyes?<br /><br />V had never been a sub before until Jane as far as we knew. He never craved pain or to be taken to the next level of an adrenaline rush. Yet here with Butch he does. He reflects before it began if that was how his subs felt. He said Jane was a poodle to his werewolfism. Really? Why if he had never been a sub before? Granted she probably couldn’t hurt him like a vamp with super strength could but it wasn’t about that with them. It was him turning over his trust which was a huge fear for him to not be in control. And recalling his reaction on his table, sweating and biting into the ball gag, he seemed like he had a breakthrough then too.<br /><br />V bi polar action. In LU he was so happy, excited to get his back cut, and Jane excited to cut it – this was the scene in her bedroom right after he freed her memories when she thought she was cracking. V or maybe it was Jane saying that it was the first time he made love to her in Lover Unleashed. I remembered him making love to her more than once in LU. For example, when he made love to her in her sleep after wiping her memory clean, when he carried her upstairs. I really don’t think he could go hard and fast at that time. And after he removed the block on her memory and he carried her to the bed and it wasn’t rough. <br /><br />V’s constant relying on Butch so much in Lover Unleashed, really sure up their relationship than V and Jane’s. Imo that was what made all the previous books, including Lover Unbound, the male and female coming to rely up on each other and building on their new foundation. Now, I see how V prefers Butch over Jane. <br /><br />It really felt scenes were out of sequence for me as though JR had dumped some scenes that should have fallen in Lover Unbound and tried to recap them in Lover Unleashed to explain the quick jump in V’s happiness. In LU, he wanted to rush to get mated – remember how excited he was to get cut? It seemed, she jumped the gun showing the “happier V” in Lover Unbound after he got Jane - Rhage picking on him in the gym (from the insider guide) and him breaking down and laughing and agreeing he was whooped; Z seeing V smiling at Jane while they were building the clinic in Father Mine. IMO if she had put the scenes from LUnl in LU prior to the penthouse scene, omitting the part with Butch and confiding into Jane, then the happy V in LUnl then it would have flowed better. My head was spinning. <br /><br />Where did Payne and Manny fit in this review? A subplot as far as I was concerned. The focus was so much on V and Jane that it was their sequel. It would have been neat, and fitting, to have V watch Payne fight. As it stands, V just took Wrath’s word on her fighting skills. Does it seem a little bizarre that V asked Butch to not be a hero and stay out of the fight but readily accepts his sister’s fighting?<br /><br />The things I deeply missed in this book that Ward has in her other books were the wonderful way she balanced action with sex, and story with emotions. So much angst. Camaraderie of the brothers? Other than V and Butch it was obsolete. This was the V/Butch/Jane – yes that order – book not Payne and Manny’s, and the discrepancies were so blatant it overpowered the rest of the story. <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16379452982986607223" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/104259236?book_show_action=true">May 25, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="UKSandy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="UKSandy" href="/user/show/3421918-uksandy">UKSandy</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3421918-uksandy?shelf=march-2011">march-2011</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer104259236&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer104259236" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6344707187729160305">Was this book worth the wait? HELL YEAH IT WAS!<br/><br/>I always knew I was going to like the next BDB book, goes without saying really and I wasn't really looking forward to Payne's book as much as the others but oh deary me how wrong was I! I wasn't really that fussed about Manny either but I JUST LOVE HIM, he is soooooo much more than I expected. He is loving, caring, considerate,HOT and that man has some talents of his own going on!<br/><br/>I loved the fact there were no lessers - What a result!!! I normally </span>
  <span id="freeText6344707187729160305" style="display:none">Was this book worth the wait? HELL YEAH IT WAS!<br /><br />I always knew I was going to like the next BDB book, goes without saying really and I wasn't really looking forward to Payne's book as much as the others but oh deary me how wrong was I! I wasn't really that fussed about Manny either but I JUST LOVE HIM, he is soooooo much more than I expected. He is loving, caring, considerate,HOT and that man has some talents of his own going on!<br /><br />I loved the fact there were no lessers - What a result!!! I normally skim the lesser bits but didn't have to this time although I was hoping to see Lash get pummelled by JM but maybe that is for another book. The band of bastards are very interesting, however, that they are still talking old worlde english when the brothers don't??? and really, they still live in a Castle and eat of pewter plates??<br /><br />Now then Payne, I just loved her, I loved her whole innocence with Manny, her enthsiasim for her new life and most of all the girl kicks ass! Her moments with V were extremely touching. Manny &amp; Payne are just great together, I'm glad the paralysis didn't last but even if it did Manny wouldn't have cared and that is why I love him.<br /><br />V oh lordy V! his sex scenes with Jane were A.M.A.Z.I.N.G!!! There were also some scenes that just pulled at those old heart strings of mine. The scene with Butch well I really felt for Butch and what a friend he is! I don't want to read of anything sexual between V &amp; Butch really, I just love them as brothers. At the end of this book I felt V is now nearly complete much more than he has been in previous books and love the fact he has now "made love" to Jane. I was really shocked to find out that they weren't mated and V didn't have her name on his back, I don't know why I didn't know this earlier! I'm really hoping we get to hear all about their mating scene in the next book as I will feel totally cheated if we don't!<br /><br />Qhuinn *sigh* Qhuinn, what to do with him, I loved the conversation with him and Layla, Qhuinn just needs someone but I also felt extremely sorry for Layla, I know people don't like her but I DO and I hope she gets the HEA I think she deserves. I also hope she is there for Qhuinn when he needs someone to talk to - that is TALK nothing else!<br /><br />Saxton - well still don't like the guy, still don't like that he is still with Blay, just doesn't work for me at all! I'm hoping Qhuinn plucks up the courage and reaches out for *his* man! Now that he has started talking to Layla I'm hoping this is the first step on that yellow brick road for Qhuinn to the lover that is his soul mate.<br /><br />The relationship between Manny &amp; Butch was just FANTASTIC, absolutely bloody brilliant, the two had me in stitches when trying to use the computer and the way Manny knocked V out of the way to get to Payne *sigh* I LOVE HIM!<br /><br />Zsadist you will always have my heart however Manny, you are bloody close, just keep in my line of sight because I got you in mine!<br /><br />I'm looking forward to finding about more about Throe, he really interested me and I want to find out what happened to his sister.<br /><br />So, again was this book worth the wait - OMFG YES, YES, YES!!!<br /><br />JRW you are soooooooooo amazing, for me you just nail it every time and you exceeded my expectations.<br /><br />This book comes 2nd after my beloved Zsadist *heart you Zsadist*</span>
  <a data-text-id="6344707187729160305" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_100873602" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/100873602" />
    <a title="Pamela / SpazP" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3522886-pamela-spazp"><img alt="Pamela / SpazP" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1413901548p2/3522886.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/100873602?book_show_action=true">May 01, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pamela / SpazP" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pamela / SpazP" href="/user/show/3522886-pamela-spazp">Pamela / SpazP</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3522886-pamela-spazp?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer100873602" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2626589174974672196"><a href='http://wickedlilpixie.com/2011/04/01/lover-unleashed-post-reading-discussion/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Originally posted at WickedLilPixie Reviews</a><br/><br/>Spaz and WLP DISCUSS:<br/>Shall we discuss? First, if you haven’t read the book: STEP AWAY FROM THE BLOG NOW. Go, RUN ALONG. I don’t want to spoil it for anyone, so CLOSE THIS NOW!<br/><br/>My Rating:<br/><br/>3.5<br/><br/>Okay. Complaints first.<br/><br/>I swear to god if I read the word Verily ONE MORE TIME, I was gonna shank a bitch. Geezus, you can say fuck but somehow you still manage to throw in verily? DURING SEX AHHHH.<br/><br/>Spaz: I would like to see Wrath pass a new law, effective immediately: T</span>
  <span id="freeText2626589174974672196" style="display:none"><a href="http://wickedlilpixie.com/2011/04/01/lover-unleashed-post-reading-discussion/" rel="nofollow noopener">Originally posted at WickedLilPixie Reviews</a><br /><br />Spaz and WLP DISCUSS:<br />Shall we discuss? First, if you haven’t read the book: STEP AWAY FROM THE BLOG NOW. Go, RUN ALONG. I don’t want to spoil it for anyone, so CLOSE THIS NOW!<br /><br />My Rating:<br /><br />3.5<br /><br />Okay. Complaints first.<br /><br />I swear to god if I read the word Verily ONE MORE TIME, I was gonna shank a bitch. Geezus, you can say fuck but somehow you still manage to throw in verily? DURING SEX AHHHH.<br /><br />Spaz: I would like to see Wrath pass a new law, effective immediately: Take the “verily”s back to the Other side, bitches!<br /><br />And the label dropping, JR Ward you are NOT going to get kick backs from the companies you mention it, so slow it down already.<br /><br />Spaz: Yeah, the name dropping is her MO and it drives me bananas! What killed me though was that Manny was speaking Brother. Is speaking Brother some kind of genetic thing??<br /><br />V. V. WTF happened to V? I think he has officially gone the way of Phury in the wtf category. All love I had for V, gone. GONE. GOOONE. What a bitch he turned out to be.<br /><br />Spaz: I was pretty much ready to help Jane pack her bags.<br /><br />Payne being paralyzed yet she is cured by super dick? COME THE FUCK ON. You so know I was going there &amp; it wasn’t going to be pretty. Male ego wet dream much? He did her so good she could walk again? BAHAHAH. No.<br /><br />Spaz: OMG I totally channeled the 50 Cent/Lil Kim song for Manny/Payne: “Magic Stick”. Look up the lyrics. That is all.<br /><br />Things Pixie is pondering:<br /><br />XCor’s buddy whatever the hell his name is, kills the human murderer…then frames Veck (Detective for it) &amp; wipes his memory. Jose (Butch’s ex-partner) hears Butch in the 911 call, thus realizing he is alive. Somehow I think these two are going to come to a head &amp; maybe the Brother’s get outted to humanity? Maybe I’m wrong, but who knows.<br /><br />Spaz: I totally agree that Jose and Butch are going to reunite somehow, that story ain’t over. Also, word out on the street (AKA the BDB messageboards) is that Veck will be the Hero in the next Fallen book, Envy.<br /><br />Why does XCor hate Wrath so much? Now that he knows the Bloodletter is not his father, watch his real father be Wrath. Cause you know Wrath’s DNA is slutty &amp; gets around more then a two dollah hoe.<br /><br />Spaz: I think that Wrath Sr. is Xcore’s dad, making Xcor and Wrath brothers. Xcore was dumped because of his “physical defect” cleft lip and the Bloodletter scooped him up. There’s nooo tellinggg what the Bloodletter told Xcore over his lifetime to make him hate Wrath… I expect a definite “keeep reeeading” from JRW on that one.<br /><br />Things Spaz is pondering:<br /><br />The Prologue mentions that the 7 Warriors fight “slayers, humans, animals and WOLFEN.” WTF are the wolfen?? And do they have anything to do with the coffins that were mentioned again, by Q when he got home from the Iron Mask?<br /><br />Pixie: Wolfen, like Wolven? Ain’t seen hide nor fur of any beasts up in Caldwell. WTF is up with the coffins, seriously! Old skool artifacts?<br /><br />Throe is in servitude to Xcore for avenging the brutal murder of his sister. He is part of the glymera society that is in the Caldwell area. And, his father was a Brother. Based on Throe’s description it does not sound like he was disowned because of “physical defects”. Was he disowned because he aligned with Xcore to have his sister avenged?? Who was his sister? And who was his father?? Would he be called Throe Sr? Aahhh!<br /><br />Pixie: I full on admit to calling Throe, Toe for the whole damn book. I have no idea why, it just looked like Toe to me. Toe Sr. I agree.<br /><br />While I don’t doubt the daughter Q has a vision of could be his and Layla’s, I do doubt the circumstances surrounding how the daughter comes to be. JRW is tricky! Does Layla spend too much time topside, goes in to her needing, then turns to Q to help her with it and thus they make baby? OR (and believe me, I like this the best) Do Qhuay get their HEA in their novella, and turn to Layla to be a surrogate mother for them?<br /><br />Pixie: OMG I am so on board with the surrogate! But verily, through artificial insemination please.<br /><br />What Pixie lurved<br /><br />Q almost killing himself as he realizes, yep I wanna tap Blays ass. I loved it! LOVED.<br /><br />Jane almost walking out on V. You go Ghost Girl, you deserved better &amp; that scene made me like her even more.<br /><br />Hollywood &amp; the popcorn machine, totally random &amp; yet I giggled.<br /><br />JR Ward dropping Dana White into a sentence, I full well know lots of people are going WHO the FUNK is Dana White. Google.<br /><br />What Spaz loved:<br /><br />The friendship that blossomed between Layla and Qhuinn. They are two peas stuck in a shitty miserable pod. He confides in her his feelings for Blay, and is honest about his lack of passion for her. He also encourages her to get out and try to find herself and what she wants. I know, it’s kumbaya shit, but I loved it. I know I know, Layla is annoying with all her “verily”s, her clingyness and the “hills are alive” singing crap when she thinks she’s in love, but she truly breaks my heart. His offer &amp; willingness to supply her with blood so she could stay topside was awesome.<br /><br />Jane. I have always been a fan of Jane and to me this was her book to show all the Jane Haters what’s up.<br /><br />OMG when Payne fights off that robber and picks him up and throws him like Superman. I was laughing out loud.<br /><br />Xcor and Throe and The Prostitute Named Kandy. I am not too proud to admit that might have been the dirrty highlight of the book for me. I was disappointed FOR her that they had to wipe her memory of that because, just, damn. &lt;–BEST part of the smexy scenes. BEST. I’d like video.<br /><br />It has to be said, I love the closure between V and Butch romantically. For me, and evidently for Jane, I’ve been worried that they would have a cheating tryst. But where their relationship went was soooo much more. What Butch did for V was just… wow. That half-breed always seems to be saving everyone!<br /><br />Pixie’s favorite line:<br /><br />“For fuck’s sake, he wished one of the SOBs would RuPaul their shift and go all feather boa and fingernail polish. But no. – Qhuinn pg. 118<br /><br />Spaz’s favorite line:<br /><br />“God, check this shit out. From slut to camp counselor in a week. Next up: a guest stint on The-fucking-View.” – Qhuinn pg. 288<br /><br />Overall<br /><br />Not bad but also not the best. I wanted more Q &amp; B, and I missed Tohr damnit. I wasn’t all into the storyline with Payne, I liked Manny a lot more then her. She verily bored me.<br /><br />There were too many storylines going on people, way too many.<br /><br />Recap:<br /><br />Manny &amp; Glory (the horse)<br />Manny &amp; Work<br />Manny &amp; Jane<br />Manny &amp; Payne<br />Manny &amp; V<br />Manny &amp; Butch<br />V &amp; Jane<br />V &amp; Payne<br />V &amp; Butch<br />Jane &amp; Payne<br />XCor &amp; his Bastards<br />XCor’s Bastard &amp; The Serial Killer (why the hell was he obsessed with that anyways?!)<br />Jose, Veck &amp; The Serial Killer<br />Jose &amp; Butch’s Voice<br />Jose &amp; Veck (Daddy issues much?)<br />XCor’s Bastard &amp; Veck<br />Spaz: 17. Hi! Me again! Let’s not forget the Xcore/Throe/Prostitute threesome! I really liked that part, OKAY? I bet her editors had a field day with that one.<br /><br />Pixie: Dear god, that’s SIXTEEN DIFFERENT POINTS PEOPLE!!! And I was told there was only 18 uses of the word Verily. I verily doubt that. And who the hell is Throe’s daddy?! WHO I ASK YOU! And yes, I totally call him Toe in my head, you know you all did too. Don’t front.<br /><br />Spaz: I called Xcor ‘Excore’ until I remembered the ‘X’ is silent. By then it was too late, so he’ll probably always be Excore now. And I want more Muhrder! We only got a taste of his crazy ass in LM and he was only mentioned once in passing.<br /><br />Pixie: I totally called him that too! He’s like X-Core…Hard Core. Okay, shutting up now.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2626589174974672196" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14048641183923819005">Reread 2020: <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ I loved all the great details I got to focus on reading this the second time around. Favorite moments: <br/><br/>-All the Manny and Payne. These are two characters I love separately, and they totally sizzle together. Payne is such a badass, in action and in dialogue. I wish that we got to see her more in later books, and hope that eventually she appears more in the series. She’s completely awesome. Manny is great and they sizzle together in their scenes. Her burning the cuffs </span></span>
  <span id="freeText14048641183923819005" style="display:none">Reread 2020: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I loved all the great details I got to focus on reading this the second time around. Favorite moments: <br /><br />-All the Manny and Payne. These are two characters I love separately, and they totally sizzle together. Payne is such a badass, in action and in dialogue. I wish that we got to see her more in later books, and hope that eventually she appears more in the series. She’s completely awesome. Manny is great and they sizzle together in their scenes. Her burning the cuffs off her wrists and slapping the hell out of Xcor at the end? Damn. <br /><br />-The torture-fest that is Qhuinn pining for Blay. Have to say the guy did it to himself, which didn’t make it any prettier to read, but JR Ward really knows how to write the angst. That scene where Saxton and Qhuinn talk and Saxton reveals to his cousin that he’s with Blay right now but doesn’t believe he’s his forever? Absolutely heartbreaking. Especially given that once again, Qhuinn drops the ball. Feel so sorry for Saxton as well. Also some great scenes with Layla. <br /><br />-BoB. This is the first book where we see them. Trying to pay more attention to these guys the second time around to pick up more nuance. Xcor I liked more than I thought I would. The others in the Band, besides Throe, who I remember liking early on and definitely liked here, came off as a bit intense particularly in that last scene with Payne, but it was only their first appearance. They have room to grow. I believe Zypher was the only one named. I enjoyed Xcor’s last scene with Payne.<br /><br />-John Matthew giving Qhuinn hell about his haircut and removing his metal. Hilarious scene!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('IJVA3FoA6bNrKO1qtEZVqEW1sKNdizuhaGuneknsBBMasykO4V4g28wDWQtDs193k+pXa5MGtcYzFeHLhK/2iQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('D9Iy3JWPd8AFjCK7eEsdDq6OKm/xesHiHZAiZdHNxBU19FsOLtG+qKKnltqPvhfReNHNpz/3T4VG7mTUHI42jw==')})
  }
